\[NOTES—1. This refers to his performance of a horse-sacrifice in the previous incarnation. For that, he was born at the outset of this cycle imbued with those thoughts and identified with the undertaking of horse-sacrifice, its factors and results.\]

——————————————————————————————

 **सोऽकामयत मेध्यं म इदꣳस्यादात्मन्व्यनेन स्यामिति। ततोऽश्वः समभवद्यदश्वत्तन्मेध्यमभूदिति तदेवाश्वमेधस्याश्वमेधत्वम्। एष ह वा अश्वमेधं वेद य एनमेवं वेद। तमनवरुध्यैवामन्यत। तꣳ संवत्सरस्य परस्तादात्मन आलभत। पशून्देवताभ्यः प्रत्यौहत्। तस्मात्सर्वदेवत्यं प्रोक्षितं प्राजापत्यमालभन्त एष ह वा अश्वमेधो य एष तपति तस्य संवत्सर आत्माऽयमग्निरर्कस्तस्येमे**



**लोका आत्मानस्तावेतावर्काश्वमेधौ। सो पुनरेकैव देवता भवति मृत्युरेवाप पुनर्मृत्युं जयति नैनं मृत्युराप्नोति मृत्युरस्याऽऽत्मा भवत्येतासां देवतानामेको भवति॥७॥ इति द्वितीयं ब्राह्मणम् ॥२॥**

 सः He अकामयत reflected, desired इति thus मे my इदम् this (swollen body) स्यात् may be मेध्यम् pure, sacrificial. अनेन through this स्याम् let (me) be आत्मन्वी embodied, corporeal. ततः so समभवन् became अश्वः the horse. यद् as अश्वत् (it) swelled तत् so अभूत् (it) became मेध्यम् इति fit for sacrifice. तत् that एव therefore (is) अश्वमेधत्वम् Ashwamedhhood अश्वमेधस्य of Ashwamedh, of horse-sacrifice. वै verily एषः he ह indeed वेद knows अश्वमेधम् the horse-sacrifice यः who वेद knows एनम् it एवम् thus. अनवरुध्य without lying down, letting remain free (unbridled) तम् it अमन्यत् thought, imagined, considered (himself as the sacrificial animal). परस्तात् after संवत्सरस्य one complete year (he) आत्मनः to himself आलभत dedicated, made an offering तम् it. देवताभ्यः to the gods पशून् animals प्रत्यौहत् gave, offered. तस्मात् therefore आलभन्ते (priests) offer प्राजापत्यम् to Prajapati प्रोक्षितम् the consecrated (horse) सर्वदेवत्यम् (dedicated) to all the gods. यः That एषः which (the sun) तपति shines वै verily एषः ह that (is) अश्वमेधः horse-sacrifice. संवत्सरः the full year (is) तस्य his आत्मा body. अयम् This अग्निः (terrestrial) fire (is) अर्कः Arka. इमे These लोकाः worlds तस्य his आत्मानः limbs. तौ Those एतौ two (fire and the sun) are अर्क-अश्वमेधौ Arka and Aswamedh, सा उ These two पुनः again भवति become एका एव just the same देवता diety, मृत्युः एव death indeed (he) अपजयति conquers, wins, पुनः-मृत्युम् further death. मृत्युः Death न not



 आप्नोति overcomes एनम् him. मृत्युः Death भवति becomes अस्य his आत्मा Self ; भवति (and) becomes एकः one एतासाम् with these देवतानाम् Gods.

——————————————————————————————

\[This is a collective meditation on the sacrificial horse and sacrificial fire as Prajapati. That the identity with Hiranyagarbha is the highest result of the Vedic rites combined with meditation is stated here\].

——————————————————————————————

 He (Hiranyagarbha) reflected thus: Let this my swollen body be sacrificed. Let me be corporeal by this body. He entered it. As the body became swollen, it became the horse. The body, on account of his entering it, became fit for sacrifice. So the horse-sacrifice gained the name of Aswamedha. Verily he who knows ¹ it thus indeed knows the horse-sacrifice. Having let the consecrated animal unbridled he considered himself as the sacrificial horse. After one complete year he dedicated it to himself and offered the other domestic and wild animals to their respective deities. Therefore priests even now dedicate Prajapati the purified animal that is offered to all the deities. The sun that shines above and illumines the universe is the horse-sacrifice; the year is his body because it is made by him. This (terrestrial) fire is Arka an accessory of sacrifice. These three worlds are the limits of the Arka. The terrestrial fire and the sun are respectively Arka



and horse sacrifice. These two² again became the one³ deity, Death. He indeed who knows⁴ this one deity is not reborn after death. Death cannot conquer him. Because he becomes the death. Being Death (Hiranyagarbha) he becomes identified with these deities.

——————————————————————————————

\[NOTES—1. One who imagines himself as the sacrificial horse and meditates thus: 'While being purified with the Mantras, I am offered to all the deities; but while being slaughtered I am offered to myself. The other domestic and wild animals are dedicated to their respective deities who are but a part of myself'.

2\. Fire and the sun, the means and the end, the sacrifice and the result.

3\. There was but one deity before. He differentiated into three ways—Action, its means and its end. After the completion of the ceremony he again becomes the single deity (death) as before. 4. As, 'I alone am Death, and none else, the horse-sacrifice and there is but only one deity identical with myself and attainable through horse and fire.'\]

——————————————————————————————

**CHAPTER ONE: SECTION THREE**

** द्वया ह प्राजापत्या देवाश्चासुराश्च। ततः कानीयसा एव देवा जायसा असुरास्त एषु लोकेष्वस्पर्धन्त ते ह देवा ऊचुर्हन्तासुरान्यज्ञ उद्गीथेनात्ययामेति॥१॥**



 प्राजापत्याः The offsprings of Prajapati ह indeed द्वया (were) of two kinds, of two classes, देवाः च the gods असुरा च and the demons. ततः Therefore, naturally देवाः the gods एव indeed (were) कानीयसाः fewer, असुराः the demons ज्यायसाः more numerous. ते They अस्पर्धन्त rivalled, vied (with each other) एषु for these लोकेषु worlds. ते ह those देवाः Gods ऊचुः said इति this हन्त well, now यज्ञे in the sacrifice अत्ययाम let (us) surpass, get the better of, असुरान् the demons उद्गीथेन by Udgithha, by loud chanting.

 The descendants of Prajapati were of two kinds, the gods and the demons.¹ Naturally the gods were few in number and the demons many.² The gods and the demons rivalled with each other for the ownership of these worlds. The gods being overwhelmed by the demons said to one another, 'Well, let us defeat the demons in the Jyotistoma sacrifice by Udgitha (loud chanting) and realize our divinity as taught in the scriptures.'

——————————————————————————————

\[NOTES.—1. The gods and the demons are the organs of speech, sight, etc., living in the body of Prajapati. The organs turn gods when they shine under the influence of thoughts and actions recommended by the scriptures. And they turn demons when they are overwhelmed by their natural thoughts and actions directed merely to secular goals. The demons take delight only in the enjoyment of their own lives.

2\. The organs are well-known to have a stronger slant for natural thoughts and actions, than to those enjoined by the scriptures. Because the former have visible results and

——————————————————————————————



are easy of accomplishment. The gods are very few, for the tendency cultivated by scriptural injunctions, being attainable with great effort, is rare. When the gods triumph, there is prevalence of merit resulting in the elevation up to Brahma-loka. When the demons win, there is preponderance of demerit resulting in the degradation down to the level of stationary objects, when there is a balance of merit and demerit, it leads to human birth.\]

 ** ते ह वाचमूचुस्त्वं न उद्गायेति तथेति तेभ्यो वागुदगायत्। यो वाचि भोगस्तं देवेभ्य आगायद्यत्कल्याणं वदति तदात्मने। ते विदुरनेन वै न उद्गात्राऽत्येष्यन्तीति तमभिद्रुत्य पाप्मनाऽविध्यन्स यः स पाप्मा यदेवेदमप्रतिरूपं वदति स एव स पाप्मा॥२॥**

 ते They (the gods) ऊचुः said to, requested वाचम् the deity presiding over Speech, the Deity identified the organ of Speech इति thus ह verily त्वम् you उद्गाय sing (chant) hymns नः for our sake. तथा इति All right, let it be so. वाक् the Deity of Speech तेभ्यः for them उद्गायत् chanted hymns. भोगः The delight, good यः that (comes) वाचि through the organ of Speech तम् that देवेभ्यः for the gods आगायत् (it) secured. तत् That यत् which कल्याणम् well, finely वदति is pronounced, is articulated आत्मने (kept) for itself. वै Verily अनेन by this उद्गात्रा the chanter अत्येष्यन्ति (they) will over, will defeat, will surpass (us) इति thus ते they (the demons) विदुः knew. (ते=they) अभिद्रुत्य charging तम् it (the chanter) पाप्मना by evil अविध्यन् pierced, touched, struck (it). सः that यः which



(is) सः that पाप्मा impurity, evil यद् एव whosoever वदति pronounces, speaks इदम् it अप्रतिरूपम् (what is) false, inelegant, improper सः That एव emphatically (is) सः that पाप्मा evil, impurity.

 The gods requested the presiding Deity of the organ of speech 'sing the hymns for our sake.' 'So be it' said the deity of the vocal organ and sang the same for the sake of the gods. Whatever delight accrues to all the organs through its instrumentality, it obtained for the gods (by singing the three hymns called Pavamana) ² but it reserved for itself the articulated speaking (fine pronunciation) (by chanting the remaining nine hymns). The demons knew well that the gods will certainly defeat them by the chanter. They rushed at the chanter and pierced him with the evil of his own attachment to sense-objects. That is emphatically that evil which is visible ³ today when one pronounces what is inelegant.⁴

——————————————————————————————

\[NOTES—1. The function of speech belongs to the deity of that organ. The organs of speech, sight, etc., are the real agents of all our activities, as well as the enjoyer of their fruits in the domain of meditation and work. The supreme self is not the doer of them. This is stated in this Upanishad in the Shruti (4.3.7). 'It thinks, as it were, it shakes as it were, etc.' This chapter also ends with the conclusion that the entire world of action, its means and results beginning with the

——————————————————————————————



Avyakrita (Undifferentiated) fall within the category of nescience. As the passage (6.5.1) of this chapter runs: 'The phenomenal universe does verily consist of name, form and action.' But the Self is beyond Avyakrita and does not consist of name, form or action.

——————————————————————————————

2.In the Jyotistoma sacrifice the chanter sings twelve hymns of which the first three are called Pavamana. The results of chanting the Pavamana go to the sacrificer while those of the remaining nine hymns go to the chanter. In the third Brahmana (28) of this chapter it is stated that the chanter gets eatable food for himself as the result of chanting the remaining nine.—Ananda Giri.

3.The evil that was injected into the organ of speech of Prajapati in his previous incarnation persists even now in the vocal organ of Prajapati's descendants.

4.Forbidden by the scriptures.\]

——————————————————————————————

** अथ ह प्राणमूचुस्त्वं न उद्गायेति तथेति तेभ्यो प्राण उदगायद्यः प्राणे भोगस्तं देवेभ्य आगायद्यत्कल्याणं जिघ्रति तदात्मने। ते विदुरनेन वै न उद्गात्राऽत्येष्यन्तीति तमभिद्रुत्य पाप्मनाऽविध्यन्स यः स पाप्मा यदेवेदमप्रतिरूपं जिघ्रति स एव स पाप्मा॥३॥**

 अथ Then ऊचुः (they) said प्राणम् to the deity of vital breath (nose) इति this ह verily त्वम् you उद्गाय chant the hymn नः for us. तथा इति So be it. प्राणः Deity of breath (nose) उदगायत् sang the hymn तेभ्यः for them. भोगः Enjoyment, good यः which (comes) प्राणे through vital breath तम् that आगायत् chanted देवेभ्यः for the gods. तत् that यद् which जिघ्रति smells



कल्याणम् well (it kept) आत्मने for itself. वै verily अनेन by this उद्गात्रा chanter (ते=they, the gods) अत्येष्यन्ति will overcome, will surpass (us) इति thus ते they (demons) विदुः knew. अभिद्रुत्य running, rushing तम् at it. (ते=they) अविध्यन् pierced charged (it) पाप्मना with evil. सः That यः which (is) सः that पाप्मा impurity, evil यद् एव whenever इदम् it जिघ्रति smells अप्रतिरूपम् (what is) bad, improper सः that (is) एव emphatically सः that पाप्मा evil.

 Then the gods spoke to the deity of vital breath (nose) : sing the hymn for our sake. The deity of life-breath said. ‘ So be it ’ and chanted the hymns for their sake. The enjoyment that accrues to all the organs through itself it secured for the gods by singing the three hymns called Pavaman, while the fine smelling it reserved for itself by singing the remaining nine hymns. The demons knew very well that the gods would overcome them by this chanter. They ran at the chanter and touched it with the evil of their own attachment to sense-objects. That is emphatically the evil which is visible today when one smells what is bad.

** अथ ह चक्षुरूचुस्त्वं न उद्गायेति तथेति तेभ्यश्चक्षुरुदगायत। यश्चक्षुषि भोगस्तं देवेभ्य आगायद्यत्कल्याणं पश्यति तदात्मने। ते विदुरनेन वै न उद्गात्राऽत्येष्यन्तीति तमभिद्रुत्य पाप्मना-**



**ऽविध्यन्स यः स पाप्मा यदेवेदमप्रतिरूपं पश्यति स एव स पाप्मा॥४॥**

 अथ Then ऊचुः (they) said, spoke to चक्षुः to the eye, presiding diety of Sight इति thus ह verily त्वम् you उद्गाय chant the hymn नः for us. तथा इति All right (said) चक्षुः diety of Sight (eyes) उद्गायत (and) chanted the hymn तेभ्यः for them, भोगः enjoyment, good यः which (comes) चक्षुषि through the eyes (sight) तम् that आगायत् secured by singing देवेभ्यः for the gods. तत् That यत् which पश्यति sees कल्याणम् well, good आत्मने (utilised) for itself. वै Verily अनेन by this उद्गात्रा chanter (ते=they, the gods) अत्येष्यन्ति will defeat, will surpass (us) इति thus ते they (demons) विदुः knew. अभिद्रुत्य rushing तम् at it अविध्यन् (they) charged (it) पाप्मना with evil. सः that यः which (is) सः that पाप्मा sin, evil यद् एव whenever इदम् it पश्यति sees अप्रतिरूपम् (what is) bad, impure सः that (is) एव emphatically सः that पाप्मा evil, impurity.

 Then the gods spoke to the presiding deity of sight—' Chant the hymn for our sake.' The deity of sight said ' All right ' and sang the hymn for them. The good that accrues from the sight to all the organs it utilised for the gods by singing the Pavamana, while the fine sight it secured for itself by singing the rest. The demons knew quite well that the gods would excell them by this chanter. They rushed at the chanter and charged him with the impurity of their own attachment to sense-objects.



That is verily the impurity which is visible today when one sees impropriety.

** अथ ह श्रोत्रमूचुस्त्वं न उद्गायेति तथेति तेभ्यः श्रोत्रमुदगायद्यः श्रोत्रे भोगस्तं देवेभ्य आगायद्यत्कल्याणꣳ शृणोति तदात्मने। ते विदुरनेन वै न उद्गात्राऽत्येष्यन्तीति तमभिद्रुत्य पाप्मनाऽविध्यन्स यः स पाप्मा यदेवेदमप्रतिरूपं शृणोति स एव स पाप्मा॥५॥**

 अथ Then ऊचुः (they) said श्रोत्रम् to the deity of hearing इति thus ह verily त्वम् you उद्गाय chant hymn नः for us. तथा इति All right (said) श्रोत्रम् the God of hearing (ears) उदगायत् (and) chanted तेभ्यः for them. भोगः Enjoyment, good यः which (comes) श्रोत्रे through hearing तम् that आगायत् chanted for, got by chanting देवेभ्यः for the gods. तत् that यत् which शृणोति hears कल्याणम् fine, well, आत्मने (utilised) for itself. वै Verily, अनेन by this उद्गात्रा chanter (ते=they, the gods) अत्येष्यन्ति will excell (us) इति thus ते they (the demons) विदुः knew. अभिद्रुत्य Rushing तम् at it (ते=they) अविध्यन् struck, charged, pierced पाप्मना with evil. यद्वेव Whenever इदम् it शृणोति hears प्रतिरूपम् (what is) improper सः that (is) एव certainly सः that पाप्मा evil, sin.

 Then the gods spoke to the presiding deity of hearing ‘Sing the hymn for our sake.’ The deity of the ears said ‘All right’ and sang the hymns for them. The delight that is derived by all the



organs through hearing it obtained for the gods by singing the Pavamana, while the fine hearing it kept for itself. The demons knew very well that the gods would overcome them by this chanter. They ran at it and charged it with the impurity of their attachment to sense-objects. That is verily the impurity which still persists when one hears wrongly.

 **अथ ह मन ऊचुस्त्वं न उद्गायेति तथेति तेभ्यो मन उदगायद्यो मनसि भोगस्तं देवेभ्य आगायद्यत्कल्याणꣳ सङ्कल्पयति तदात्मने। ते विदुरनेन वै न उद्गात्राऽत्येष्यन्तीति तमभिद्रुत्य पाप्मनाऽविध्यन्स यः स पाप्मा यदेवेदमप्रतिरूपꣳ सङ्कल्पयति स एव स पाप्मैवमु खल्वेता देवताः पाप्मभिरुपासृजन्नेवमेनाः पाप्मनाऽविध्यन्॥६॥**

 अथ Then ऊचुः (they) said, spoke to मनः to the deity of mind इति thus ह verily त्वम् you उद्गाय sing the hymn नः for us. तथा इति All right (said) मनः the mind (and) उद्गायत chanted the hymn तेभ्यः for them. भोगः Enjoyment, delight यः which (comes) मनसि through the mind त्वम् that (it) आगायत् chanted for, secured by chanting देवेभ्यः for the gods यत् which सङ्कल्पयति (it) thinks कल्याणम् well तत् that आत्मने (kept) for itself. वै Verily (ते=they, the gods) अनेन by this उद्गात्रा chanter अत्येष्यन्ति will excell, will surpass (us) इति thus ते they, (demons) विदुः knew. अभिद्रुत्य Rushing तम् at it (ते=they) अविध्यन् charged, overwhelmed पाप्मना with evil.



यद्वेव whenever इदम् it सङ्कल्पयति thinks अप्रतिरूपम् (what is) ill, wrong सः that (is) एव indeed सः that पाप्मा impurity, evil. एवम् उ Likewise, in this way खलु also (ते=they) उपास्तृजन् tainted, touched एताः these, other, देवताः deities पाप्मभिः with evil एवम् thus अविध्यन् injected, perced एताः these (deities) पाप्मना with evil (sin).

 Then the gods spoke to the Deity of the mind — ‘Chant the hymns for our sake.’ ‘So be it’ said the mind and sang the hymn for them. The delight that issues of the mind to all the organs, it obtained for the gods by chanting the Pavamana while the fine thinking it reserved for itself by chanting the rest. The demons knew well that through this chanter the gods would excel them. They rushed at it and charged it with the evil of their own attachment to sense-objects. That is the evil which persists today when one thinks wrongly. In this way they also tainted other deities ¹ with evil, that is to say, pierced them with evil.

——————————————————————————————

\[NOTES—1. The skin and the rest that have not been mentioned.

The gods were thus led to the conclusion that the deities presiding over the organs are incapable of chanting the hymns, because the latter contracted evil owing to their attachment for fine results. Hence they are not to be meditated upon in order to transcend death. The gods became helpless.\]

——————————————————————————————



** अथ हेममासन्यं प्राणमूचुस्त्वं न उद्गायेति तथेति तेभ्य एष प्राण उदगायत्ते विदुरनेन वै न उद्गात्राऽत्येष्यन्तीति तदभिद्रुत्य पाप्मनाऽविध्यन्स यथाऽश्मानमृत्वा लोष्टो विध्वꣳसेतैवꣳहैव विध्वꣳसमाना विष्वञ्चो विनेशस्ततो देवा अभवन्पराऽसुरा भवत्यात्मना पराऽस्य द्विषन्भ्रातृव्यो भवति य एवं वेद॥७॥**

 अथ Then ऊचुः (they) said इमम् to this प्राणम् vital power, life आसन्यम् sitting in the mouth इति thus ह verily त्वम् you उद्गाय chant the hymn नः for us. तथा इति All right (said) एषः this प्राणः vital power, life उद्गायत (and) chanted the hymn (for them). वै Verily (ते they) अनेन by this उद्गात्रा chanter अत्येष्यन्ति will excell, will surpass (us) इति thus ते they विदुः knew. अभिद्रुत्य Rushing तम् at it (ते=they) पाप्मना with evil, impurity, taint अविध्यन् wanted to pierce (it). यथा As ऋत्वा striking, hitting अश्मानम् against a rock, hard stone, adamant लोष्टः a ball of mud, a clod of earth विध्वंसेत is dashed to pieces, is shattered to atoms एवम् so, in this way (ते=they) ह एवं indeed विध्वंसमानाः flung विष्वञ्चः in all directions, in many ways विनेशः perished. ततः Therefore देवाः Gods अभवन् became (fire etc), असुराः demons (अभवन्= became) पराः (=पराभूताः) destroyed, crushed यः who (the sacrificer of to-day) एवम् thus, similarly (like the ancient sacrificer) वेद knows भवति becomes आत्मना (his true self) द्विषन् inimical, envious भ्रातृव्यः kinsmen भवति is परास्य killed, crushed.



 \[The results of the meditation on the vital force is stated here. The vital force being the common self of the body as well as the sense-organs is to be resorted to as one's self to get rid of the false identity.\] .

 Then the gods spoke to the life-force having its seat in the oral cavity—' Sing the hymn for our sake.' ' So be it ' said the vital power to the gods and sang the hymns for them. The demons were quite aware that by this chanter the gods would overcome them. They rushed at it and desired to pierce it with the impurity of their own attachment to sense-objects. But as a ball of earth is dashed to pieces when hurled upon a rock, so they were crushed to atoms and destroyed being scattered in many ways. Owing to the destruction of demons, their enemies the gods became their divine-selves, fire ¹ and so forth, and the demons perished. In this manner ² the sacrificer of today who realises his identity with the vital force like the ancient sacrificer becomes his true self as Prajapati and his inimical kinsmen ³ are routed.

——————————————————————————————

\[NOTES—1. Formerly also they had been fire and so on but this awareness of their real natures was hidden by the taint of their natural attachment to sense-objects as they had identified themselves with body alone. On the cessation of that evil, they gave up their false identification with the body

——————————————————————————————



and realised their identity with fire etc., as taught by the scriptures.

——————————————————————————————

2.As the sacrificer of a past age mentioned in this Vedic allegory tested the deities presiding over the sense-organs, discarded them as stricken with the taint of attachment to sense-objects, identified himself with the taintless vital force and thereby getting rid of the evil was identified with Prajapati, so the sacrificer of today will restore by the same procedure his lost identity with vital force or Prajapati.

3.The impurity that obstructs the attainment of his true self as Prajapati. A kinsman is also sometimes friendly, as, for instance, Bharat the half-brother of Rama.\]

——————————————————————————————

** ते होचुः क्व नु सोऽभूद्यो न इत्थमसक्तेत्यमास्येऽन्तरिति सोऽयास्य आङ्गिरसोऽङ्गानाꣳ हि रसः॥८॥**

 ह A particle of surprise ते they, the gods ऊचुः said नु with deliberation इति thus क्व where अभूत् was सः he यः who असक्त restablished, restored नः us इत्थम् thus. अयम् It (is) अन्तरम् within आस्ये इति the mouth. सः It अयास्यआङ्गिरसः Ayasya Angiras हि for (सः it) रसः (is) the essence, self अङ्गानाम् of limbs, of organs.

 The gods (the organs of Prajapati) deliberated with surprise thus—' Where was it who has thus re-established us in our real stations and then decided.'¹ It is that vital force also resides within the mouth. It is called Ayasya ² Angirasa ³ for it is well known to the self ⁴ of the body and the limbs.



——————————————————————————————

\[NOTES—1. Realised it within themselves.

2\. The vital force was perceived by them as being present within themselves without assuming any particular form, it is called Ayasya.

3\. Since it did not assume any particular form, it restored the organs to their real nature. Hence it is called Angirasa (literally, the self of the limbs).

4\. Because without it they dry up and die.\]

——————————————————————————————

** सा वा एषा देवता दूर्नाम दूरꣳ ह्यस्या मृत्युर्दूरꣳ ह वा अस्मान्मृत्युर्भवति य एवं वेद॥९॥**

 सा That वै verily एषा this देवता deity नाम called, celebrated दूः Dur distant, हि for मृत्युः death (is) दूरम् far, remote, away अस्याः from it. यः Who एवम् thus वेद knows अस्मात् from him मृत्युः death वै verily भवति is, remains दूरम् far, distant.

 That verily is this deity ¹ celebrated as Dur Distant because death is away ² from it. Death ³ is away from him who knows ⁴ the vital force in this way.

——————————————————————————————

\[NOTES—1. It is this deity in the present sacrificer's body whom the gods realised as their saviour.

2\. The vital power being ever unattached does not contract evil of attachment to sense-objects by the contact with the sense-organs of which it is the Self, unlike one who touching another who has touched a corpse becomes impure. Anandagiri.

3\. Death is evil of attachment to sense-objects.

——————————————————————————————



——————————————————————————————

4.Meditates upon the vital power free from the evil of attachment. Meditation means a mental approach to the form of the deity or the like as prescribed by the scriptures and concentration on it, to the exclusion of all conventional notions, till complete identification with it as with one's own body is attained. For, this Upanishad (4.1.2) says ' Being a god, he attains the gods.' The Shruti also says, ' one becomes exactly the same as one meditates upon.' (Shatapatha Brahman. P. V. 2. 20.)

——————————————————————————————

** सा वा एषा देवतैतासां देवतनां पाप्मानं मृत्युमपहत्य यत्राऽऽसां दिशामन्तस्तद्गमयाञ्चकार तदासां पाप्मनो विन्यदधात्तस्मान्न जनमियान्नान्तमियान्नेत्पाप्मानं मृत्युमन्ववायानीति॥१०॥**

 सा That वै verily एषा this देवता deity अपहत्य having taken away मृत्युम् death पाप्मानम् evil एतासाम् of these देवतानाम् gods गमयाञ्चकार went तत् there यत्र where (there is) अन्तः end आसाम् of these दिशाम् quarters, directions. तत् There (it) विदधात् left, deposited आसाम् their पाप्मनः evils, sins. तस्मात् Therefore न not इयात् (one) should approach (associate) जनम् a person, न not इयात् should go, should be अन्तम् end, border (of that region) नेत् lest (one) अन्ववायानि इति imbibes contract पाप्मानम् impurity, evil मृत्युम् death.

 Verily this deity removed ¹ death ², the impurity of these gods, carried them to the end ³ of these directions ⁴, east, west, etc., and deposited ⁵ them there. Therefore let no one associate with a person of that territory or be to that



territory beyond the border, lest he should contract that impurity which is as bad as the death.

——————————————————————————————

\[NOTES—1. Their identification with the vital force kept off the evil from them.

2\. One's degradation is due to one's attachment with the sense-objects as prompted by natural ignorance. Hence this evil of attachment is as bad as death.

3\. End means the territory inhabited by people holding views contradictory to the Vedas, as the forest is spoken of to be the end of the inhabited territory.

4\. The directions are to mean that part of the country peopled by the possessors of the Vedic knowledge.

5\. Placed in many insulting ways among the people of the country beyond the border who do not identify themselves with the vital force. The evil is born of the contact of the senses with their respective objects. Hence it must dwell in some animal being.\]

——————————————————————————————

** सा वा एषा देवतैतासां देवतानां पाप्मानं मृत्युमपहत्याथैना मृत्युमत्यवहत्॥११॥**

 सा That वै verily एषा this देवता deity अपहत्य removing, taking away मृत्युम् death पाप्मानम् evil, taint एतासाम् of these देवतानाम् gods अथ next, then अत्यवहत् carried एनाः them (the gods) मृत्युम् beyond death.

 This deity removed death—the impurity ¹ of these gods, and then carried the gods beyond death.



——————————————————————————————

\[NOTES—1. The impurity of attachment is death to the gods as it limited them to their bodies and made them forget their unlimited divine forms. That impurity is destroyed by the identification with the vital force. Hence the latter is the destroyer of that impurity.\]

——————————————————————————————

** स वै वाचमेव प्रथमामत्यवहत्सा यदा मृत्युमत्यमुच्यत सोऽग्निरभवत्सोऽयमग्निः परेण मृत्युमतिक्रान्तो दीप्यते॥१२॥**

 सः It (the vital power) वै verily अत्यवहत् carried वाचम् the organ of speech एव only प्रथमाम् the first. यदा When सा it अत्यमुच्यत delivered, dissociated, freed मृत्युम् from death सः it अभवत् became अग्निः fire. सः That अयम् this अग्निः fire अतिक्रान्तः having gone beyond, having transcended मृत्युम् death दीप्यते shines, परेण beyond reach.

 Verily the vital power carried first¹ the organ of speech across death. When the latter had been delivered from death it became fire.² That fire having transcended death is luminous beyond its reach.

——————————————————————————————

\[NOTES—1. Because it is a better chanter of hymns than other organs.

2\. It became what it had been before with this difference that before its deliverance it was not as luminous as now.\]

——————————————————————————————

** अथ प्राणमत्यवहत्स यदा मृत्युमत्यमुच्यत स वायुरभवत्सोऽयं वायुः परेण मृत्युमतिक्रान्तः पवते॥१३॥**



 अथ Then अत्यवहत् (it) carried प्राणम् the organs of nose. यदा When सः it अत्यमुच्यत transcended मृत्युम् death सः it अभवत् became वायुः air. सः That अयम् this वायुः air अतिक्रान्तः having got rid of, having liberated from मृत्युम् death पवते blows परेण beyond (its) reach.

 Then the organ of nose was carried across death. When the former transcended death, it became (what it had been before) air. That air being liberated from death blows beyond its reach.

** अथ चक्षुरत्यवहत्तद्यदा मृत्युमत्यमुच्यत स आदित्योऽभवत्सोऽसावादित्यः परेण मृत्युमतिक्रान्तस्तपति॥१४॥**

 अथ Then अत्यवहत् (it) carried चक्षुः the organ of vision. यदा When तत् it अत्यमुच्यत went beyond, transcended मृत्युः death सः it अभवत् became आदित्यः the Sun. सः That असौ this आदित्यः Sun अतिक्रान्तः having got rid मृत्युम् of death तपति shines, burns, परेण beyond (its) reach.

 Then the organ of vision was taken across death. When it was dissociated from death, it became (what it had been before) the sun. That sun being freed from death burns beyond its reach.

** अथ श्रोत्रमत्यवहत्तद्यदा मृत्युमत्यमुच्यत दिशोऽभवꣳस्ता इमा दिशः परेण मृत्युमतिक्रान्ताः॥१५॥**

 अथ Then अत्यवहत् (it) took across, श्रोत्रम् the organ of hearing. यदा When तत् it अत्यमुच्यत got rid of, transcended



मृत्युम् death ताः they अभवन् became दिशः quarters. ताः Those इमाः these दिशः directions अतिक्रान्ताः having gone across मृत्युम् death परेण beyond (its) reach.

 Then the organ of hearing was taken across death. When the former was freed from death, it became (what it had been before) the directions. Those directions having got rid of death remain (divided into the east and so forth) beyond its reach.

 **अथ मनोऽत्यवहत्तद्यदा मृत्युमत्यमुच्यत स चन्द्रमा अभवत्सोऽसौ चन्द्रः परेण मृत्युमतिक्रान्तो भात्येवꣳ ह वा एनमेषा देवता मृत्युमतिवहति य एवं वेद॥१६॥**

 अथ Then अत्यवहत् (it) carried मनः the mind. यदा When तत् it अत्यमुच्यत transcended मृत्युम् death सः it अभवत् became was transformed into चन्द्रमा the moon. सः That असौ this चन्द्रमा the moon अतिक्रान्तः having got rid मृत्युम् of death भाति shines परेण beyond (its) reach. यः Who वेद knows एवम् thus, एवं ह so वै verily एषा this देवता deity अतिवहति carries, takes एनम् it मृत्युम् across death.

 Then the mind was taken across death. When the former transcended death, it became (what it had been before) the moon. That moon having become free from death shines beyond its reach. So verily one, who knows thus, the vital force as including the five sense-organs is carried beyond death by this deity.



** अथाऽऽत्मनेऽन्नाद्यमागायद्यद्धि किञ्चान्नमद्यतेऽनेनैव तदद्यत इह प्रतितिष्ठति॥१७॥**

 अथ Then आगायत् (it) chanted for, secured by chanting अन्नाद्यम् eatable food आत्मने for itself. हि Because यत् किं च whatever अन्नम् food अद्यते is eaten तत् that अद्यते is eaten अनेन by it (vital force) एव alone. इह on that प्रतितिष्ठति (it) rests, subsists.

 \[The vital power first chanted the Pavamana and secured the result—the identity with Prajapati—to be shared by the five organs.\]

 Then it obtained eatable food for its own sake by chanting the remaining nine hymns in order to live in the body. Whatever food is eaten by the creatures in the world the same is eaten by the vital force alone. It subsists on that food when the latter is transformed into the body.

 **ते देवा अब्रुवन्नेतावद्वा इदꣳ सर्वं यदन्नं तदात्मन आगासीरनुनोऽस्मिन्नन्न आभजस्वेति ते वै माऽभिसंविशतेति तथेति तꣳ समन्तं परिण्यविशन्त। तस्माद्यदनेनान्नमत्ति तेनैतास्तृप्यन्त्येवꣳ ह वा एनꣳ स्वा अभिसंविशन्ति भर्ता स्वानाꣳ श्रेष्ठः पुर एता भवत्यन्नादोऽधिपतिर्य एवं वेद य उ हैवंविदँ स्वेषु प्रति प्रतिर्बुभूषति न हैवालं भार्येभ्यो भवत्यथ य एवैतमनुभवति यो वैतमनु भार्यान्बुभूषति स हैवालं भार्येभ्यो भवति॥१८॥**



 ते Those देवाः gods अब्रुवन् spoke, said—सर्वम् All इदम् this यत् which अन्नम् food (there is) वै only, just एतावत् this much. तत् That आगासीः (you) acquired, appropriated आत्मने for yourself. अनु Now अस्मिन् in this अन्ने food आभजस्व give share नः to us इति thus. ते You वै verily अभिसंविशत sit around, surround मा इति me. तथा इति All right. समन्तम् Around तम् it परिण्यविशन्त sat down. तस्मात् Hence यत् whatever अन्नम् food अनेन by this (vital force) अत्ति (one) eats तेन by that एताः these (gods) तृप्यन्ति are satisfied. यः Who वेद knows एवम् thus एनम् him वै ह verily एवम् in this way स्वाः kinsmen, relatives अभिसंविशन्ति sit around, surround. भवति (He) is, remains भर्त्ता supporter, maintainer स्वानाम् of his relatives, श्रेष्ठः best, greatest एताः to them पुरः in the fore-front, अन्नादः eater of food, अधिपतिः master, ruler. यः ह उ Who, that one स्वेषु of his relatives प्रति-बुभूषति desires to rival, tries to compete एवं विदम् प्रति with one such (knower), (सः he) न not हि एव certainly भवति becomes अलम् enough, capable भार्येभ्यः (to support) the dependants. अथ But यः एव who indeed अनुभवति follows एतम् him वा or यः who अनु under एतम् him बुभूषति desires to maintain भार्यान् dependants सः he एव ह indeed भवति becomes अलम् capable भार्येभ्यः (of supporting) dependants.

 The gods¹ (the organs of speech, etc.) spoke to the vital force—"Whatever food is eaten in the world to sustain life is only so much and no more and you have appropriated it all for your use by chanting. Therefore make us also sharers of the food that is for yourself." Then the vital force



commanded them to sit surrounding him. The gods agreed and sat down encircling him. Hence whatever food is partaken of by the vital force satisfies² these gods (the organs). As the organs did with vital force so do his relatives sit around facing him who knows the vital force as the support of the organs. He becomes the refuge of his relatives, the best among them, and remains in their fore-front as the vital force was of the organs. Further being free from disease he becomes a good partaker of food and the sole protector of them. That one among his relatives who wants to rival a knower of the vital force is incapable to maintain his dependants like the demons. But one who follows such a knower or wants to support one's dependants under him is alone capable of doing so and none else.

——————————————————————————————

\[NOTES—1. The organs are called gods as they bring their respective objects to light.

2\. Nourishes. The organs have no independent connection with food. The food eaten by the vital force nourishes them.\]

——————————————————————————————

**सोऽयास्य आङ्गिरसोऽङ्गानाꣳ हि रसः प्राणो वा अङ्गानाꣳ रसः प्राणो हि वा अङ्गानाꣳ रसस्तस्माद्यस्मात्कस्माच्चाङ्गात्प्राण उत्क्रामति तदेव तच्छुष्यत्येष हि वा अङ्गानाꣳ रसः॥९॥**



 सः That अयास्य आङ्गिरसः Ayasya Angirasa रसः (is) essence, sap, self, हि indeed अङ्गानाम् of the limbs, members (of the body). प्राणः The vital force वै verily रसः (is) the essence, self अङ्गानाम् of the members. हि For प्राणः the vital power वै verily रसः sap, self अङ्गानाम् of the limbs. तस्मात् Therefore यस्मात् कस्मात् च from whichever अङ्गात् limbs, part प्राणः vital force उत्क्रामति departs, deserts, तत् that एव indeed तत् that शुष्यति dries up, withers. हि Because एषः that वै of course in truth रसः sap अङ्गानाम् of the limbs.

 \[In the eighth paragraph vital force has simply been called Ayasya Angiras. The following text makes a specific statement why it is so called.\]

 The vital force is called Ayasya Angirasa, the self indeed of the parts (of the body). It is indeed the sap of the parts. It is verily their self. Therefore any part of the body which is deserted by the vital force dries up. It is in truth the self of the body as well as the organs. (As the organs live through the vital power, the former are to be left out and the latter is to be meditated upon.)

** एष उ एव बृहस्पतिर्वाग्वै बृहती तस्या एष पतिस्तस्मादु बृहस्पतिः॥२०॥**

 एषः This (vital power) उ एव (is) indeed, also बृहस्पतिः Brihaspati. वाक् The speech वै verily (is) बृहती Brihati. एषः



This (is) तस्याः its पतिः protector, lord. तस्मात् उ Therefore (this is) बृहस्पतिः Brihaspati.

 \[The following texts extol vital power as the self of the Vedas and magnifies it as the self of all in order to show that it is the proper object of meditation.\] This vital power called Angirasa is indeed Brihaspati. The speech verily is the Brihati ¹ metre that has thirty-six syllables. The vital force is the lord of speech, that is, of the Riks in the form of Brihati metre which includes all Riks. Therefore this is Brihaspati, viz., the self of the Riks.

——————————————————————————————

\[NOTES—1. According to Taittiriya Samhita (V. i. 3. 5) ' the metre Anustubha is speech.' And this metre is included in the metre Brihati. Hence the speech is called Brihati.\]

——————————————————————————————

** एष उ एव ब्रह्मणस्पतिर्वाग्वै ब्रह्म तस्या एष पतिस्तस्मादु ब्रह्मणस्पतिः॥२१॥**

 एषः This (the vital force) उ एव indeed (is) ब्रह्मणस्पतिः the lord of Brahman. वाक् Speech वै verily (is) ब्रह्म Brahman (yajus). एषः This (is) तस्याः its पतिः lord. तस्मात् उ Therefore (this is) ब्रह्मणस्पतिः lord of Brahman.

 This vital power is indeed lord of Brahmana or yajus which is a particular kind of speech. The



speech is verily Brahman (yajus) and the vital force is its lord. Therefore this is the Lord of Brahmana.

 **एष उ एव साम वाग्वै सामैष सा चामश्चेति तत्साम्नः सामत्वम्। यद्वेव समः प्लुषिणा समो मशकेन समो नागेन सम एभिस्त्रिभिर्लोकैः समोऽनेन सर्वेण तस्माद्वेव सामाश्नुते साम्नः सायुज्यꣳ सलोकतां य एवमेतत्साम वेद॥२२॥**

 एषः This (vital force) उ एव indeed, also साम (is) Saman. वै Verily वाग् speech (is) सा Sa (she) एषः this (is) अमा Amā. सा च Sa (she) अमः च and Ama इति because (it is) तत् that (is) सामत्वम् the reason of being called Saman साम्नः of Saman. वा or यद् एव as (सः it) समः (is) equal प्लुषिणा to an ant or worm समः equal मशकेन to a mosquito, to a gnat समः equal नागेन to an elephant, समः equal एभिः to these त्रिभिः three लोकैः worlds, समः equal अनेन सर्वेण to all this (Universe). तस्मात् Therefore (सः it) वै एव indeed साम (is) Saman. यः Who वेद knows एतत् this साम Saman एवम् thus, as such अश्नुते (he) gets, attains सायुज्यम् identify, union सलोकताम् existence in the same world साम्नः of Saman.

 This vital power is indeed sāman. Verily speech is sā¹ (she) and the vital force is Ama.¹ The reason of its being called saman is that it is a combination of speech and the vital power—Sa and Ama. Or else the vital force is Saman because it is equal² to the body of a worm, equal to the size



of a gnat, equal to the form of an elephant, equal to these three worlds (i.e., the body of the Viraj), equal to this Universe (i.e., the form of Hiranya-garbha). He who knows this vital power called Saman (as endowed with the glories revealed by the Vedas) obtains either identification with the same body and organs as the vital power or existence in the same world with it according to the difference in meditation.

——————————————————————————————

\[NOTES—1. Sa and Ama refer to all objects denoted by feminine and masculine words respectively.

2\. It is present in its fullness in those bodies as the main characteristics of a cow exist in each cow. The vital force being formless and all-pervasive it cannot be only of the size of these bodies. The equality does not merely mean just filling up those bodies by contraction or expansion like lamp-light in a jar or room. A formless and all-pervasive principle can easily assume particular forms in different bodies.\]

——————————————————————————————

** एष उ वा उद्गीथः प्राणो वा उत्प्राणे हीदꣳ सर्वमुत्तब्धं वागेव गीथोच्च गीथा चेति स उद्गीथः॥२३॥**

 एषः This (Vital power) उ वा also उद्गीथः (is) Udgitha. प्राणः Life, Vital force (is) वै verily उत् ut, support. हि For सर्वम् all इदम् this (Universe) उत्तब्धम् (is) held aloft प्राणेन by the vital power. वाक् The speech एव indeed गीथा (is) Githa, a form of Sound उत् च ut च and गीथा Githa इति because सः this (is) उद्गीथः Udgitha, a division of the Saman.



 This vital power is also Udgitha, a particular division of the Saman. It is verily Ut (support), as it supports all this universe. The Speech is indeed Githa, a variety of sound. Because it is Ut and Githa, it is Utgitha.

 **तद्धापि ब्रह्मदत्तश्चैकितानेयो राजानं भक्षयन्नुवाचायं त्यस्य राजा मूर्धानं विपातयताद्यदितोऽयास्य आङ्गिरसोऽन्येनोदगायदिति वाचा च ह्येव स प्राणेन चोदगायदिति॥२४॥**

 तत् On this (subject) अपि even, also ह it has been said : ब्रह्मदत्तः Brahmadatta (by name) चैकितानेयः a descendant of Chaikitana भक्षयन् drinking, taking राजानम् Soma-juice उवाच said इति this अयम् this राजा Soma-juice विपातयतात् may strike off, may cut off त्यस्य (=तस्य) his (my) मूर्धानम् head, यत् if अयास्य आङ्गिरसः Ayasya Angirasa उद्गायत् chanted hymn अन्येन by anyone else इतः other than this. हि For सः च he एव indeed उद्गायत् च इति chanted the hymn प्राणेन by vital power.

 On this subject this narrative is told in the Shruti : Brahmadatta, a descendant of Chaikitana, while drinking soma juice in a sacrifice took the oath—Let this Soma juice in the bowl cut off my head if I entertain this lie that Ayāsya Āngirasa sang hymn by any deity other than this vital power combined with speech. Indeed the chanter sang the hymns by speech ¹ and the vital force.



 **तस्य हैतस्य साम्नो यः स्वं वेद भवति हास्य स्वं तस्य वै स्वर एव स्वं तस्मादार्त्विज्यं करिष्यन्वाचि स्वरमिच्छेत तया वाचा स्वरसम्पन्नयाऽऽर्त्विज्यं कुर्यात्तस्माद्यज्ञे स्वरवन्तं दिदृक्षन्त एव अथो यस्य स्वं भवति भवति हास्य स्वं य एवमेतत्साम्नः स्वं वेद॥२५॥**

 यः Who वेद knows स्वम् ornament, wealth तस्य of that एतस्य of this साम्नः Saman अस्य his स्वम् wealth ह indeed भवति increases. वै Verily तस्य its स्वम् wealth एव indeed स्वरः sweet tone, musical voice तस्मात् therefore करिष्यन् in order to do आर्त्विज्यम् duty of a priest इच्छेत (one) should wish स्वरम् musical tone वाचि in voice, कुर्यात् (he) should do, should perform आर्त्विज्यम् priestly functions तया by that वाचा voice, स्वर-सम्पन्नया enriched with a fine tone. तस्मात् Therefore यज्ञे in a sacrifice एव indeed दिदृक्षन्तः (people) desirous to see स्वरवन्तम् (ऋत्विजम्) a priest, endowed with a cultured voice. अथ Just as यस्य whose स्वम् wealth भवति is, increases. यः Who एवम् thus वेद knows स्वम् the wealth. साम्नः If Saman अस्य his स्वम् wealth ह indeed भवति is, increases.

 He who knows the ornament of this Saman (the vital power) indeed obtains wealth. Sweet voice is verily its ornament (wealth). Therefore one who wishes to do the duties of a priest should be desirous of culturing ¹ musical note in his voice.



in order to enrich the Saman with it. He should perform his priestly functions through that cultured voice embellished with a sweet tone. Therefore in a sacrifice, people desire to look for a priest having sweet voice, as they long to see a wealthy man. He who knows the wealth of Saman as such indeed attains wealth.

——————————————————————————————

\[NOTES—1. Appropriate means for culturing a rich voice are cleaning the teeth and sipping oil, etc.\]

——————————————————————————————

 ** तस्य हैतस्य साम्नो यः सुवर्णं वेद भवति हास्य सुवर्णं तस्य वे स्वर एव सुवर्णं भवति हास्य सुवर्णं य एवमेतत्साम्नः सुवर्णं वेद॥६॥**

 यः Who वेद knows सुवर्णं the gold, wealth तस्य of that (mentioned before) एतस्य of this साम्नः Saman अस्य his सुवर्णं gold भवति increases ह indeed. वै Verily स्वरः good tone एव indeed (is) तस्य its सुवर्णं gold, wealth. यः Who वेद knows एतत् this सुवर्णं gold साम्नः of Saman एवम् as such तस्य its सुवर्णं gold ह indeed भवति is, increases.

 He who knows what is the gold (wealth) of this Saman verily attains gold. Good tone is indeed its gold (wealth). He who knows what is the gold (wealth) of Saman verily attains gold.

——————————————————————————————

\[NOTES—1. Correct sound in obedience to the rules of phonetics.\]

——————————————————————————————



** तस्य हतस्य साम्नो यः प्रतिष्ठां वेद प्रति ह तिष्ठति तस्य वै वागेव प्रतिष्ठा वाचि हि खल्वेव एतत्प्राणः प्रतिष्ठितो गीयतेऽन्न इत्यु हैक आहुः॥२७॥**

 यः Who वेद knows प्रतिष्ठाम् the support तस्य of that एतस्य of this साम्नः Saman ह indeed प्रतितिष्ठति is supported. वै Verily वाक् speech, root of the tongue and other parts of the body एव indeed (is) तस्य its प्रतिष्ठा resting place, support. हि For खलु indeed एव that एतत् this प्राणः life, vital power प्रतिष्ठितः rests, is established वाचि on speech गीयते is transformed into a chant, assumes the form of a chant. एके Some ह indeed आहुः say, श्ने इति उ (resting) on food.

 He who knows speech on which this Saman rests gets a support. Speech (root of the tongue and other parts of the body) verily is its resting place. For resting on the root of the tongue and other places the vital force indeed is transformed into a chant. It is held by some that resting on food it becomes a chant.

** अथातः पवमानानामेवाभिसेहः। स वै खलु प्रस्तोता साम प्रस्तौति स यत्र प्रस्तुयादेतानि जपेत्। असतो मा सद्गमय तमसो मा ज्योतिर्गमय मृत्योर्माऽमृतं गमय इति। स यदाहार्सतो मा सद्गमयेति मृत्युर्वा असत्सदमृतं मृत्योर्माऽमृतं गमयामृतं मा कुर्वित्येवैतदाह तामसो मा ज्योतिर्गमयेति मृत्युर्वै तमो ज्योतिरमृतं मृत्यो-**



**र्माऽमृतं गमयामृतं मा कुर्वित्येवैतदाह मृत्योर्माऽमृतं गमयेति नात्र तिरोहितमिवास्ति। अथ यानीतराणि स्तोत्राणि तेष्वात्मनेऽन्नाद्यमागायेत्तस्मादु तेषु वरं वृणीत यं कामं कामयेत तꣳ स एष एवं विदुद्गाताऽऽत्मने वा यजमानाय वा यं कामं कामयते तमागायति तद्धैतल्लोकजिदेव न हैवालोक्यताया आशाऽस्ति य एवमेतत्साम वेद॥२८॥**

 अथ Now अतः therefore अभ्यारोहः ascension, repetition एव only पवमानानाम् of the hymns called Pavamana. वै Verily सः that प्रस्तोता priest called Prastota खलु indeed प्रस्तौति mutters, recites the hymns. यत्र While सः he प्रस्तुयात् recites (it) तत् then एतानि these (mantras) जपेत् should be muttered, should be repeated—गमय make go, lead मा me सत् to good असतोः from evil. तमसः From darkness गमय take, lead मा me ज्योतिः to light मृत्योः from death, गमय carry, lead मा me अमृतम् इति to immortality. यत् When सः it (the mantra) आह says. गमय lead मा me असतोः from evil सत् इति to good मृत्युः death (is) वै verily असत् evil, सत् good (is) अमृतम् immortality. एव Indeed एतत् it (mantra) आह says मृत्योः from death गमय cause to go, lead मा me अमृतं to immortality. कुरु make मा me अमृतम् इति immortal. (When the mantra says) तमसः from darkness गमय lead मा me ज्योतिः इति to light, तमः darkness (is) वै verily मृत्युः death, ज्योतिः light (is) अमृतम् to immortality ; एव Indeed एतत् it (mantra) आह says : मृत्योः from death गमय lead मा me अमृतम् to immortality, कुरु make मा me अमृतम् इति immortal. अत्र Here, in this hymn मृत्योः from death गमय lead मा me अमृतम् इति



to immortality, (the meaning is) न not अस्ति is, lies इव like, as तिरोहितम् hidden. अथ Then यानि whichever, those इतराणि other, remaining स्तोत्राणि hymn आगायेत् should chant for तेषु in them अन्नाद्यम् eatable food आत्मने for his own. तस्मात् उ Therefore (the sacrificer) वृणीत ask for तेषु in them, in those hymns वरम् boon, blessing तम् whichever यम् that कामयेत (he) desires. सः That एषः this एवं विद् such a knower उद्गाता chanter, यम् whichever कामम् desires कामयेत् desires तम् that आगायन्ति attains, gets आत्मने for himself वा or यजमानाय for the sacrificer ह indeed तत् that एतत् this (meditation) एव alone लोक-जित् (is) the conqueror of the world. यः Who वेद knows एतत् this साम Saman (vital force) एवम् as such एव ह verily अस्ति there is न not आशा hope, possibility अलोकयतायाः unfitness for the world, deprivation of the world.

 Now therefore the recitation (Abhyaroha 1) of only the Pavamana hymns is defined. Verily Prastotri priest indeed chants the hymns. At the time of chanting them, let him mutter these three yajus mantras. "Take me from evil 2 to good 3. Take me from darkness 4 to light 5. Take me from death to immortality." In the first mantra: 'Take me from evil to good,' 'evil' is verily death and 'good' is immortality. So the second mantra: 'Take me from death to immortality' means render me immortal. In the third mantra: 'Take me from darkness to light' 'darkness' is verily death and 'light' is immortality. The mantra:



'Take me from death to immortality' means make me immortal. In the mantra: "Take me from death to immortality," the sense does not appear to be obscure. Then the chanter should obtain the eatable food for his own self by singing the other hymns. Therefore, when the remaining hymns are sung the performer should choose a blessing whichever he wants. Whatever desire the chanter endowed with such knowledge may desire for his own self or for the performer he accomplishes them by that recital. This meditation on vital power alone does enable one to attain the world of Hiranyagarbha even if it is separated from rites. He who meditates upon the vital force called Saman till he realises his identity with it has no fear of being deprived of the world of Hiranyagarbha (the cosmic form of vital force).

——————————————————————————————

\[Notes—1. Abhyaroha is a ceremony which consists in the recitation of three yajus. It is so called because it grants elevation (ascent, Abhyaroha) to the performer to the realisation of his innate divinity.

2\. Our natural thoughts and actions are evil as they degrade us very much.

3\. Our actions and thoughts that are prompted by the scriptures are good as they lead to divinity.

4\. Ignorance is darkness, being of the nature of a veil. It again is death, as it is the cause of death.\]

——————————————————————————————



——————————————————————————————

5.Light means immortality. Knowledge being luminous is called light. That knowledge being of imperishable nature is called immortality.

6.Enable me to realise the divine status of Viraj. The import of the first mantra is: Enable me to be identified with the means of realisation. While the import of second one is: Enable me to transcend that even, it being a kind of nescience and attain identity with the result. The third combines the meanings of both.

7.Because he is already in that world, one who is already in a village is never eager to reach it like one who is in the forest.\]

——————————————————————————————

**CHAPTER ONE: SECTION FOUR**

 **आत्मैवेदमग्र आसीत्पुरुषविधः सोऽनुवीक्ष्य नान्यदात्मनोऽपश्यत्सोऽहमस्मीत्यग्रे व्याहरत्ततोऽहन्नामाभवत्तस्मादप्येतर्ह्यामन्त्रितोऽहमयमित्येवाग्र उक्त्वाऽथान्यन्नाम प्रब्रूते यदस्य भवति स यत्पूर्वोऽस्मात्सर्वस्मात्सर्वान्पाप्मन औषत्तस्मात्पुरुष ओषति ह वै स तं योऽस्मात्पूर्वो बुभूषति य एवं वेद॥१॥**

 अग्रे In the beginning, before (creation), Prior to (manifestation) इदम् this (Universe) आसीत् was एव verily आत्मा Self, not different from the body of Viraj पुरुषविधः like a human form. सः He (Viraj) अनुवीक्ष्य looking around, reflecting (on himself and his features) अपश्यत् found, beheld न not अन्यत् anything आत्मनः than himself. अहम् I अस्मि



am सः he (Viraj) इति thus अग्रे first व्याहरत् uttered, said. ततः Therefore अभवत् became अहं नाम named I. तस्मात् Therefore अपि even एतर्हि to this time आमन्त्रितः the inquired one, the addressed one अग्रे first उक्त्वा saying अयम् it (is) अहम् इति I अथ then प्रब्रूते says अन्यत् the other नाम name यत् which भवति is, belongs अस्य to him. यत् As, because सः He (Viraj) पूर्वः first अस्मात् of this सर्वस्मात् all. औषत् burnt, consumed सर्वान् all पाप्मनः sins, evils, तस्मात् therefore पुरुषः Purush, one who burnt first. यः Who वेद् knows, realises एवम् thus सः he वै ह verily ओषति burns, consumes तम् him यः who बुभूषति wishes to obtain पूर्वः before, in advance अस्मात् him (the sage).

 Prior to manifestation this universe of various bodies was not verily different from the body of Viraj which is like a human form having a head, the hands, etc. Viraj¹, the first embodied being, looked in all directions and beheld nothing else but himself consisting of body and organs. He first declared²—I am Viraj. Hence even now when anyone amongst men is enquired he first describes himself as I (i.e., identified with Viraj), and then pronounces the other name (such as Devdatta and Yajnadatta) that belongs to him. Viraj in his past incarnation was the first of all the aspirants to consume all evils that obstruct the attainment of the state of Viraj, he is called Purusha (one who consumed first). He, who attains this knowledge



thus indeed consumes him, who wishes to be Viraj in advance of him.

——————————————————————————————

\[NOTES—1. Viraj and Hiranyagarbha are the subtle and gross forms respectively of the same being.

2\. Declaration was prompted by the impression of his past life which was purified by Vedic knowledge.\]

——————————————————————————————

** सोऽबिभेत्तस्मादेकाकी बिभेति स हायमीक्षां चक्रे यन्मदन्यन्नास्ति कस्मान्नु बिभेमीति तत एवास्य भयं वीयाय कस्माद्ध्यभेष्यद्वितीयाद्वै भयं भवति॥२॥**

 सः He (Viraj) अबिभेत् feared, got afraid. तस्मात् Therefore एकाकी one (when) alone बिभेति fears, gets afraid. सः He अयम् this (Viraj) चक्रे made ईक्षाम् deliberation, reflection यत् if, because ह a mere particle न not अस्ति there is अन्यत् any other मत् than me कस्मात् from whom नु then बिभेमि do (I) fear इति thus. ततः Then, after that एव only अस्य his भयम् fear वीयाय departed, left. हि Because, for कस्मात् from whom अभेष्यत् did (he) fear ? वै certainly भयम् fear भवति is, comes द्वितीयात् from a second, from a rival.

 Viraj feared just like us on account of a false notion about his extinction. Therefore one still fears when one is alone. Viraj deleberated—If there is no second entity other than myself to be my rival, whom I fear? (For there is none to kill me). From that deliberation (right knowledge of the self) his fear departed. Because whom was



he to fear? Fear certainly comes from a second entity.

** स वै नैव रेमे तस्मादेकाकी न रमते स द्वितीयमैच्छत्। स हैतावानास यथा स्त्रीपुमाꣳसौ सम्परिष्वक्तौ स इममेवाऽऽत्मानं द्वेधाऽपातयत्ततः पतिश्च पत्नी चाभवतां तस्मादिदमर्धबृगलमिव स्व इति ह स्माऽऽह याज्ञवल्क्यस्तस्मादयमाकाशः स्त्रिया पूर्यत एव ताꣳ समभवत्ततो मनुष्या अजायन्त॥३॥**

 सः He (Viraj) वै verily न not एव at all रेमे was happy, felt delight. तस्मात् Therefore एकाकी one (when) lonely न not रमते feels delight. सः He (Viraj) ऐच्छत् desired द्वितीयम् a second (a mate). सः He ह indeed आस became एतावान् so much in extent, as large यथा as स्त्री-पुमांसौ woman and man सम्परिष्वक्तौ in embrace. सः He अपातयत् made to fall, parted द्वेधा into two इयम् this एव very आत्मानम् body. ततः From that अभवताम् became पतिः च husband पत्नीच and wife. तस्मात् Therefore याज्ञवल्क्यः Yajnavalkya, Son of Yajnavalkya आह स्म said इदम् this (body) (is) इव like स्व अर्धवृगलम् इति half of a pea (or shell) स्व of oneself. तस्मात् Therefore अयम् this आकाशः Sky, void, body of man पूर्यते is filled स्त्रिया by wife एव indeed. समभवत् (he) embraced, coupled with, united. ताम् with her (daughter). ततः From that मनुष्याः men अजायन्तः were born.

 Verily Viraj did not at all feel any delight on account of loneliness. Therefore one even today



does not feel any delight when one is lonely. He longed for a second, a mate. Being of an infallible will he became of the size of a man and wife in embrace. He then divided that enlarged body into two parts. From that division husband and wife came into being. So Yajnavalkya said—this body of man is the half of himself like the half of a split pea. He married a wife. Since the one half of a man is a void without a wife, man indeed becomes full when he has a wife. Viraj called Manu was united with his daughter named Satarupa. From that union men were born.

** सा हेयमीक्षां चक्रे कथं नु माऽऽत्मन एव जनयित्वा सम्भवति हन्त तिरोऽसानीति सा गौरभवदृषभ इतरस्ताꣳ समेवाभवत्ततो गावोऽजायन्त वडवेतरावभवदश्ववृष इतरो गर्दभीतरावगर्दभ इतरस्ताꣳ समेवाभवत्तत एकशफमजायताजेतराऽभवद्वस्त इतरोऽविरितरा मेष इतरस्ताꣳ समेवाभवत्ततोऽजावयोऽजायन्तैवमेव यदिदं किञ्च मिथुनमा पिपीलिकाभ्यस्तत्सर्वमसृजत॥४॥**

 उ ह Verily सा She (Satarupa) चक्रे made इयम् this इच्छाम् reflection, deliberation. हन्त Alas कथम् how सम्भवति (he) couples मा with me जनयित्वा having given birth to, having created एव only आत्मनः from himself ? नु Now असानि इति let me तिरः disappear, conceal. सा She अभवत् became गौः a cow, इतरः the other (manu) ऋषभः a bull, समभवत् coupled was united ताम् एव with her. ततः From that (union)



गावः kine अजायन्त were born. इतरा The one अभवत् became, assumed the form of वडवा a mare, इतरः the other अश्ववृषः a stallion ; इतरा the one (Satarupa) गर्दभी femal ass ; इतरः the other (Manu) गर्दभः male ass समभवत् was united एव only ताम् with her. ततः From that (union) एकशफम् the class of one-hoofed animals (e.g. horses, mules and asses) अजायत was born. इतरा The one (Satarupa) अभवम् became, turned into अजा she-goat, इतरः the other (Manu) बस्तः he-goat. इतरा The one (Satarupa) अविः ewe, इतरः the other (Manu) मेषः a ram, समभवत् joined एव only ताम् with her. ततः From that (joining) अज-अवयः goats and sheep अजायन्त were born. एवम् In this way, by this process एव only असृजत् (he) created, produced सर्वम् all तत् that इदम् this यत् किं च whatever (exists) मिथुनम् in pairs आ upto, down to पिपीलिकाभ्यः the ants.

 Satarupa verily reflected thus: How he can do this vile act of coupling with me after having given birth to me from his own self? Now let me conceal myself by changing into another species. Thinking thus she assumed the form of a cow. Then Manu turned into a bull and was united with her. From that union kine came into existence. Satarupa became a mare, and Manu a stallion. Similarly the former became a female ass, and the latter becoming a male ass was joined with her. From that joining the three species of one-hoofed animals—horses, mules and asses were born. Satarupa changed herself into a she-goat



and Manu a he-goat. The former became a ewe and the latter becoming a ram was united with her. From that union goats and sheep were born. By this process only they created all that exists in pairs as male and female down to the ants i.e., the entire animate world.

** सोऽवेद्हं वाव सृष्टिरस्म्यहꣳ हीदꣳ सर्वमसृक्षीति ततः सृष्टिरभवत्सृष्ट्याꣳ हास्यैतस्यां भवति य एवं वेद॥५॥**

 सः The (Viraj) अवेत् knew, was conscious अहम् I अस्मि am वाव indeed सृष्टिः creation. हि Because अहम् I असृक्षि created, projected इति thus. ततः Therefore, hence अभवत् (he) became, was called सृष्टिः creation. यः Who वेद knows, realises एवम् as such, as identified with, ह indeed भवति (he) is becomes (a creator) एतस्याम् in this सृष्ट्याम् creation (of Viraj), world.

 After creating this universe Viraj was conscious : I am indeed this created universe; because I created all this and it is not different from me. Hence he was called creation. He, who like Viraj knows this universe as identified with himself becomes creator in this world.

** अथेतत्स्यभ्यमन्थत्स मुखाच्च योनेर्हस्ताभ्यां चाग्निमसृजत तस्मादेतदुभयमलोमकमन्तरतोऽलोमका हि योनिरन्तरतः। तद्यदिदमाहुरमुं यजामुं यजेत्येकैकं देवमेतस्यैव सा विसृष्टिरेष उ ह्येव**



**सर्वे देवाः। अथ यत्किञ्चेदमार्द्रं तद्रेतसोऽसृजत तदु सोम एतावद्वा इदꣳ सर्वमन्नं चैवान्नादश्च सोम एवानमग्निरन्नादः सैषा ब्रह्मणोऽतिसृष्टिः। यच्छ्रेयसो देवानसृजताथ यन्मर्त्यः सन्नमृतानसृजत तस्मादतिसृष्टिरतिसृष्ट्याꣳ हास्यैतस्यां भवति य एवं वेद॥६॥**

 अथ Then अभि-अमन्थत् churned, rubbed इति thus. सः he (Viraj) असृजत् created अग्निम् fire योनेः from (its) source मुखात् च from mouth च and हस्ताभ्याम् from two hands. तस्मात् Therefore एतद् this उभयम् both (are) अन्तरतः within, at the inside अलोमकम् hairless. हि Because योनिः female organ अन्तरतः at the inside अलोमका without hair. तत् Then यत् when आहुः (the priests) say इदम् this: यज sacrifice अमुम् to this, यज sacrifice अमुम् to the other (Indra), देवम् God एक-एकम् one after another, separately एतस्य of him एव only (is) सा this विसृष्टिः special creation, supreme manifestation. हि Because एषः he (Viraj) उ एव indeed (is) सर्वे all देवाः the gods. अथ Now यत्किं च whatever इदम् this (is) आर्द्रम् wet, liquid तत् that असृजत (he) created रेतसः from semen. तत् उ That (liquid) सोमः (is) Soma. वै Verily सर्वम् all इदम् this (Universe) एतावत् (is) this much अन्नं च food अन्नादः च and the eater of food एव only. सोमः Soma एव indeed (is) अन्नम् food, अग्निः fire अन्नादः the eater of food. सा That एषा this अति-सृष्टिः Supreme creation ब्रह्मणः of Brahman (Viraj) यत् that असृजत (he) created देवान् Gods श्रेयसः superior (to him). अथ Now यत् because सन् being मर्त्यः mortal असृजत् created अमृतान् immortals, gods तस्मात् therefore अति-सृष्टिः (this is) supreme creation. यः (He) who वेद knows एवम् as



such भवति becomes a (creator) एतस्याम् in this अति सृष्ट्याम् Supreme creation, Universe अस्य ह of it (Viraj).

 After creating this world consisting of pairs, Viraj churned his mouth by putting his hands into it and thus created fire from its source—his mouth and his hands. Therefore both of them are hairless within just as a female organ is without hair inside.

 Thinking that the gods are different on account of the differences of their names, hymns, functions, etc., when the priests at the time of performing sacrifice say—offer oblations to fire, offer oblations to Indra and so on—they are mistaken ; since the special creation of gods is out of himself. He himself has become manifested as ail these gods. Now whatever is liquid in this world he created from his own semen. That liquid called semen is Soma. This universe is verily this much—food and the eater of food only, and nothing more. Soma is food and fire the eater of food. This is the supreme creation of Viraj. Because he created the gods who are even superior to him. Although he was a mortal he created immortals, the gods. Therefore this is a supreme creation. He who regards this universe consisting of fire and soma as identical with himself becomes Viraj the cosmic life in this supreme creation.



\[He created similarly from other limbs other gods. Indra from the arms, Vasus from the thigh, and Pushan from the feet.\]

** तद्धेदं तर्ह्यव्याकृतमासीत्तन्नामरूपाभ्यामेव व्याक्रियतसौनामाऽयमिदꣳरूप इति तदिदमप्येतर्हि नामरूपाभ्यामेव व्याक्रियतेऽसौनामाऽयमिदꣳ रूप इति स एष इह प्रविष्टः। आ नखाग्रेभ्यो यथा क्षुरः क्षुरधानेऽवहितः स्याद्विश्वम्भरो वा विश्वम्भरकुलाये तं न पश्यन्ति। अकृत्स्नो हि स प्राणन्नेव प्राणो नाम भवति। वदन्वाक्पश्यꣳश्चक्षुः शृण्वञ्श्रोत्रं मन्वानो मनस्तान्यस्यैतानि कर्मनामान्येव। स योऽत एकैकमुपास्ते न स वेदाकृत्स्नो ह्येषोऽत एकैकेन भवत्यात्मेत्येवोपासीतात्र ह्येते सर्वम् एकं भवन्ति। तदेतत्पदनीयमस्य सर्वस्य यदयमात्माऽनेन ह्येतत्सर्वं वेद। यथा ह वै पदेनानुविन्देदेवं कीर्तिꣳ श्लोकं विन्दते य एवं वेद॥७॥**

 तत् That (causal state of the Universe) इदम् this (differentiated universe) तर्हि then (before manifestation) आसीत् was अव्याकृतम् indifferentiated, unmanifested. तत् It (causal Universe) व्याक्रियत developed, differentiated नाम-रूपाभ्याम् through name and form एव only. अयम् It असौ नाम that-named, called so and so इदं रुप इति this-formed, such and such form. तत् so अपि even एतर्हि now, to this day इदम् it, an undifferentiated object व्याक्रियते is differentiated नाम-रूपाभ्याम् through name and form. अयम् It असौ नाम of such name, इदं रुपम् इति of this form. सः That एषः this (self)



प्रविष्टः has entered (into these bodies) आ upto नख-अग्रेभ्यः the tips of the nails, nail-ends. यथा Just as क्षुरः a razor, स्यात् is अवहितः contained, put क्षुरधाने in the razor-case. barber's instrument-bag, वा or विश्वम्भरः fire, which sustains the universe विश्वम्भर-कुलाये in the source (wood) of Vishwambhara, तम् It न not पश्यन्ति (they) see, realise हि because सः it (is) अकृत्स्नः incomplete, conditioned प्राणन् एव doing the functions of life भवति (It) is प्राणनाम called life, वदन् speaking वाक् Speech (speaker) पश्यन् seeing चक्षुः the eye (seer), शृण्वन् hearing श्रोत्रम् the ear (listner), मन्वानः thinking मनः the mind (thinker). तानि Those एतानि these (life etc.) एव merely अस्य its कर्म-नामानि name according to function. सः He यः who उपास्ते worships, meditates upon एक-एकम् each one अतः of these सः he न not वेद knows ; हि because एषः it (is) अकृत्स्नः incomplete, conditioned अतः is these भवति is एक-एकेन by particular function. आत्मा इति Supreme Self एव alone उपासीत is to be meditated upon, worshipped हि because अत्र in It (unconditioned self) सर्वे all एते these (differences) भवन्ति are, become एकी united, one, अस्य of it सर्वस्य all तत् that एतत् this यत् which (is) अयम् this आत्मा self पदनीयम् is to be realised, known हि because वेद (one) knows एतत् this सर्वम् all अनेन through it. यथा ह एवम् Just as अनुविन्देत् (one) gets back, finds (a missing animal) पदेन through foot-prints, hoof-marks यः (He) who वेद knows एवम् this (as free from differentiations) विन्दते attains, obtains कीर्त्तिम् fame, knowledge of unity श्लोकम् (and) association (with relatives), liberation.

 That¹ this universe was undeveloped before manifestation. Causal universe developed of itself



into name and form. It got some name (such as Devadatta or Yajnadatta) and had some form (say, white or black). So even now when an undeveloped thing is developed into name and form, it gets some name and has some form. The supreme self has entered² into all these bodies from Hiranyagarbha down to a clump of grass, up to the very end of the nails just as in the world a razor lies in the barber's instrument-bag or as fire which sustains the universe lies in wood. They do not realise self in its true nature although they see its conditioned aspect that performs the following functions. When It performs breathing, It is called Life (as one is called a cutter or cook).³ When It speaks, It is called speaker. When It sees, It is called the seer. When It hears, It is called the listner. When It thinks, It is called the Thinker. Life, mind, etc. are merely its names in respect of the functions it performs. He who meditates singly upon each one of these particular aspects does not know the self as a whole,⁴ because It is conditioned by being divided into these single characteristics (from the totality of aspects). The supreme Self alone is to be meditated upon, because all these differences due to limiting adjuncts, such as life etc. become one in the unconditioned self, just as different reflections of the sun in water



become one in the sun. Of all these, this entity called self alone is to be known and nothing else. Because one knows all these when the self is known, just as in the world one finds a missing animal. He who realises the self as free from all differentiations attains the knowledge of unity and liberation.

 ——————————————————————————————

\[NOTES—1. It means ‘that which was this and this which was that’ indicating an identity of the universe in the causal and kinetic states. As foam appears on limited water so the causal state passes into the kinetic. It shows clearly that a non-existing thing cannot be produced or an existent thing cannot be lost. As the existence of a tree in the seed-form is inferred from the sprout, so is the causal state of the universe inferred from its kinetic state.

2. The aim of the Upanishads is to teach about the self upon which the limitations of agent, action and result have been superimposed by primordial ignorance. The entrance of the self into these bodies is like the reflection of the sun in water.

3\. Likewise the self is called the doer, the goer, etc. according to the functions performed through hands, feet, etc.

4\. As long as one knows the self as possessed of the natural functions of seeing, hearing, etc. he does not really know the whole (real) self.

5\. The self appears conditioned through innate ignorance just as a mother of pearl appears as a piece of silver or sky is imagined concave or blue through error. Self-realisation means the removal of this ignorance, which is possible by the awareness of the real self. Self-knowledge therefore is not an

——————————————————————————————



action which is the product of ignorance like the birth of a son in dream. The teachers of Self-knowledge frequently make use of the following parable to show the illusory nature of our sorrows and sufferings consequent upon the bondages of body, etc. Once ten persons crossed a river. Reaching the other bank one of them counted their number to ascertain the safe arrival of all. And he was sorry to find that one of them was lost. Each one of them counted the number with same result, for every counter omitted himself through ignorance. So they all started lamenting. A traveller passing that way enquired about the matter and understood the whole situation in no time. He asked one of them to count again. When the latter counted nine, the former telling him to stop said, ‘you are the tenth.’ This procedure he carried on with all the ten men. When they realised their mistake, they became very happy and their sorrows vanished.\]

 **तदेतत्प्रेयः पुत्रात्प्रेयो वित्तात्प्रेयोऽन्यस्मात्सर्वस्मादन्तरतरं यदयमात्मा। स योऽन्यमात्मनः प्रियं ब्रुवाणं ब्रूयात्प्रियꣳ रोत्स्यतीतीश्वरो ह तथैव स्यादात्मानमेव प्रियमुपासीत स य आत्मानमेव प्रियमुपास्ते न हास्य प्रियं प्रमायुकं भवति॥८॥**

 तत् That एतद् this (self) प्रेयः (is) dearer पुत्रात् than a son, प्रेयः(= प्रियतरः) dearer वित्तात् than wealth, प्रेयः dearer सर्वस्मात् than all अस्मात् others (objects), अयम् this यत् which (is) आत्मा Self अन्तरतरम् (is) nearer, inner. सः He यः who ब्रूयात् should say ब्रुवाणम् to one calling अन्यम् auything else प्रियम् dearer आत्मनः than self, प्रियम् (his) dear (one) रोत्स्यति\*

——————————————————————————————

\*Literally ‘will meet with extinction of life.’–Nityananda.

——————————————————————————————



इति will perish ह certainly. ईश्वरः (He is) capable, competent, स्यात् (it) shall be एव indeed तथा so (true), उपासीत (one) should meditate एव only आत्मानम् upon self प्रियम् (as) dear. सः He यः who उपास्ते meditates एव only आत्मानम् upon self प्रियम् as dear ह certainly अस्य his प्रियम् dear one भवति is न not प्रमायुकम् mortal, short-lived.

 \[Here is another reason why the supreme self should be chosen as the only object of meditation to the exclusion of everything else.\]

 This self is dearer than a son who is held extremely dear in the world. It is dearer than wealth such as gold or jewels. It is dearer than all other external objects that are held dear in life. It is nearer than even the body and the organs. It is innermost. If one who holds the self as dear say to one calling anything else dearer than the self, what is dear to you will perish—he is indeed capable of saying so, and what he said will certainly be true. Therefore one should meditate upon the self alone as dear. Of him who meditates upon the self as dear, his dear ones are not mortal.

——————————————————————————————

\[NOTES—1. Mortal objects cannot attain immortality but they attain longer life by virtue of this meditation.— Anandagiri.\]

——————————————————————————————

 ** तदाहुर्यद्ब्रह्मविद्यया सर्वं भविष्यन्तो मनुष्या मन्यन्ते। किमु तद्ब्रह्मावेद्यस्मात्तत्सर्वमभवदिति॥९॥ **



 तत् That आहुः (They, some speakers) say, declare यत् which (is) ब्रह्मविद्यया by the knowledge of Brahman (supreme self) भविष्यन्तः (we) shall become, shall attain identify with सर्वम् all,—(इति thus) मनुष्याः men मन्यन्ते think, hold. किमु what तद् that ब्रह्म Brahman अवेत् knew यस्मात् by which तत् It अभवत् became सर्वम् इति all.

 \[That the aim of the whole Upanishad is to impart the knowledge of Brahman is introduced here.\]

 Some seekers declare: Men having special aptitude for the knowledge of Brahman hold that this knowledge is sure to lead to identity with all excluding nothing. Well, what did that Brahman know by which It attained identity with all?

 ** ब्रह्म वा इदमग्र आसीत्तदात्मानमेवावेत्। अहं ब्रह्मास्मीति। तस्मात्तत्सर्वमभवत्तद्यो यो देवानां प्रत्यबुध्यत स एव तदभवत्तथर्षीणां तथा मनुष्याणां तद्धैतत्पश्यन्नृषिर्वामदेवः प्रतिपेदेऽहं मनुरभवꣳ सूर्यश्चेति तदिदमप्येतर्हि य एवं वेदाहं ब्रह्मास्मीति स इदꣳ सर्वं भवति तस्य ह न देवाश्च नाभूत्या ईशते। आत्मा ह्येषाꣳ स भवति अथ योऽन्यां देवतामुपास्तेऽन्योऽसावन्योऽहमस्मीति न स वेद यथा पशुरेवꣳ स देवानाम्। यथा ह वै बहवः पशवो मनुष्यं भुञ्ज्युरेवमेकैकः पुरुषो देवान्भुनक्त्येकस्मिन्नेव**



**पशावादीयमानेऽप्रियं भवति किमु बहुषु तस्मादेषां तन्न प्रियं यदेतन्मनुष्या विद्युः॥१०॥**

 वै Verily, emphatically अग्रे before, prior to (realisation) इदम् this (self perceived in the body) आसीत् was ब्रह्म Brahman. तत् It अवेत् knew आत्मानम् Itself एव only इति thus अहम् I अस्मि am ब्रह्म Brahman Ultimate Reality. तस्मात् Therefore तत् It अभवत् became सर्वम् all, यः यः whoever देवानाम् among the Gods प्रति-अबुध्यत् knew, comprehended तत् It सः he एव also अभवत् became तत् that (Brahman) तथा Similarly ऋषीणाम् among the sages, तथा similarly मनुष्याणाम् among-men. ऋषि The sage वामदेवः named Bamadeva पश्यत् seeing, realising एतत् this तत् ह (as) That प्रतिपेदे knew अहम् I अभवम् became मनुः Manu सूर्यः च इति and the sun. अपि Even एतर्हि now, to this day यः whoever वेद knows, realises एवम् thus तत् It इदम् this इति thus अहम् I अस्मि am ब्रह्म Brahman. सः He भवति becomes सर्वम् all इदम् this (Universe). च ह Even देवाः the Gods न not ईशते are able to do तस्य his अभूत्यै harm. हि Because सः he भवति becomes एषाम् their आत्मा Self. अथ Again, on the other hand सः he (one, ignorant of Brahman) यः who उपास्ते adores, worships अन्याम् another देवताम् God इति thus असौ He (is) अन्यः one (differentiated from me) अहम् I अस्मि am अन्यः another (subordinate to him) न not वेद knows, यथा as सः he (is) एव indeed पशुः an animal देवाणाम् of the Gods. वै Verily यथा ह as बहवः many पशवः animals भुज्ञ्ज्युः (= भोजयेयुः) feed, serve मनुष्यम् man एवम् so एकः एकः each one मनुष्यः man भुनक्ति (= भोजयति) feeds, pleases देवान् Gods एव only एकस्मिन् पशौ in a single animal



आदीयमाने being given भवति (if) becomes अप्रियम् unpleasant किमु what बहुषु of many (animals). तस्मात् Therefore तत् It (is) न not प्रियम् pleasant एषाम् to them यत् that मनुष्याः men विद्युः should know तत् That.

 This self that is perceived in the body was emphatically Brahman and all even before realisation.It knew only Itself as immediate and direct Brahman, and with this knowledge It became all this universe. And those of the gods who realised It in this manner became Brahman. Similarly whoever among the sages and men had this realisation also became That. The sage named Vamdeva knowing his own Self as identical with Brahman visualised these mantras: ‘I was Manu and the Sun, etc.’ And even now whoever in the similar way knows the identity of his self and Brahman becomes all this Universe. Even the powerful gods, much less others, are incapable of doing any harm to a knower of Brahman as he has become their Self. On the other hand an ignorant person who adores another god thinking ‘He is different from me and I am his subordinate’ does not know truth. This man being ignorant of Brahman is like an animal to the gods. As in the world cows and horses serve their owner and controller, so does the ignorant man serve the gods. Even the loss of one animal is painful to one who has many such.



One can well imagine what anguish it causes him who is robbed of many animals. Therefore the gods get mortified if men get out of their grip and somehow realise this identity of the Self and Brahman.

——————————————————————————————

\[NOTES—1. This knowledge of Brahman is never obs- cured in any state of differentiation. Brahman cannot be otherwise under any condition of time, space and causation. The same Reality cannot be Brahman and not-Brahman at the same time just as the seen cannot be both bright and dark; or a woman cannot be half-old and half-young at one time.

2. As a cow or other animals are useful to men by yielding milk or carrying loads so this man is useful to the gods for doing sacrifices and other services.—Rig Veda (4. 26. 10.)

3\. There is no difference regarding the knowledge of Brahman, between giants like Vamadeva and the human weaklings of to-day. Knowers of Brahman whether they are men, gods or sages are same, for they are all one with Brahman. The Shruti verily says that a knower of Brahman becomes Brahman.

4\. So Vyasdev says in the Anugita, ‘The world of the gods, O Arjun, is filled with those who perform rites and gods do not like that mortals should surpass them.’ (Mahabharat, 14. 20. 59).\]

——————————————————————————————

 **ब्रह्म वा इदमग्र आसीदेकमेव तदेकꣳ सन्न व्यभवत्। तच्छ्रेयोरूपमत्यसृजत क्षत्त्रं यान्येतानि देवत्रा क्षत्त्राणीन्द्रो वरुणः सोमो रुद्रः पर्जन्यो यमो मृत्युरीशान इति। तस्मात्क्षत्त्रात्परं**



**नास्ति तस्माद्ब्राह्मणः क्षत्त्रियमधस्तादुपास्ते राजसूये क्षत्त्र एव तद्यशो दधाति सैषा क्षत्त्रस्य योनिर्यद्ब्रह्म। तस्माद्यद्यपि राजा परमतां गच्छति ब्रह्मैवान्तत उपनिश्रयति स्वां योनिं य उ एनꣳ हिनस्ति स्वाꣳ योनिमृच्छति स पापीयान्भवति यथा श्रेयाꣳसꣳ हिꣳसित्वा॥११॥**

 अग्रे Before इदम् this (the Kshatriyas and the other castes) आसीत् was, identical with. वै verily ब्रह्म Brahman, Viraj एकम् one एव only. तत् He सन् being एकम् alone (without a protector) such as a Kshatriya न not व्यभवत् prospered, flourished. तत् He अत्यसृजत् created श्रेयः grand, excellent रुपम् form. क्षत्रम् the Kshatriya,–यानि those एतानि who (are) क्षत्राणि Kshatriyas देवत्रा among the gods, इन्द्रः Indra the king of Gods, वरुणः Varuna ( god of aquatic animals), सोमः the Moon (god of the Brahmanas), रुद्रः Rudra (god of the beasts), पर्जन्यः Parjanya (god of lightning etc.), यमः Yama (god of the manes), मृत्युः death (god of diseases), ईशानः इति (and) Ishana (god of luminaries). तस्मात् Therefore अस्ति there is न no (one) परम् higher, better, क्षत्रात् than the Kshatriyas: तस्मात् Hence ब्राह्मणः the Brahmana उपास्ते worships, praises क्षत्रियम् the Kshatriya अधस्तात् from below, from a lower seat राजसूये in the Rajasuya (sacrifice), दधाति (He) gives, offers तत् that यशः fame, homage क्षत्रे on the Kshatriya एव indeed. सा That एषा this यत् which (is) ब्रह्म the Brahman योनिः is the source क्षत्रस्य of the Kshatriya. तस्मात् Therefore यदि-अपि although राजा the king गच्छति gets, attains परमताम् superiority distinction अन्ततः at the end उपनिश्रयति salutes ब्रह्मे the



Brahman एव indeed स्वाम् his योनिम् his source. सः He यः उ who हिनस्ति slights, hurts एनम् it ऋच्छति strikes, destroys स्वाम् at his योनिम् source. सः He भवति becomes पापीयान् worse sinner, more wicked तथा as (one) हिंसित्वा injuring, slighting श्रेयांसम् (one's) superior.

 Before the creation of the Kshatriya and other castes verily Viraj was alone. Being without a protector in the form of a Kshatriya he did not prosper in his work. He created an excellent form, the Kshatriyas, who are well known in the world as Kshatriyas among the gods: Indra, king of the gods, Varuna, god of the aquatic animals, the moon, god of the Brāhmans, Rudra, god of the beasts, Parjanya, god of the lightning, etc., Yama, god of the Manes, Death, god of the diseases, etc., and Ishan, god of luminaries. Therefore there is none superior to the Kshatriya, because they are endowed with special eminence. Hence the Brahman praises the Kshatriya from a lower seat in the Rajsuya sacrifice. He offers that homage to the Kshatriya. The Brahman is the source of the Kshatriya, therefore although the king gets the distinction of being anointed in the sacrifice, when the ceremony is over he salutes the Brāhman, his source. He who looks down upon the Brāhman destroys his own source. He becomes more wicked



by doing this, as in life one grows worse by hurting one's superior.

——————————————————————————————

\[NOTES—1. Viraj in the form of fire is the deity of Brahmana. He is called Brahman because he identifies himself with the Brahman caste.

2\. After them, the human Kshatriyas, Pururavas and those who belong to the lunar and solar dynasties, presided over by Indra and other Kshatriya gods, were also created.

3\. When the king, anointed for the Rajsuya sacrifice addresses the priest from his seat as ‘Brahman’, the latter replies, ‘You, O king are Brahman’.\]

——————————————————————————————

** स नैव व्यभवत्स विशमसृजत यान्येतानि देवजातानि गणश आख्यायन्ते वसवो रुद्रा आदित्या विश्वे देवा मरुत इति॥१२॥**

 एव Yet, even now, सः he (Viraj) न not व्यभवत् increased, flourished. सः He असृजत् created विशम् Vaishya एतानि those यानि who देवजातानि the class (the species) of gods आख्यायन्ते are mentioned, are designated गणशः in groups:—वसवः (eight) Vasus, रुद्राः (eleven) Rudras आदित्याः (twelve) Adityas विश्वेदेवाः (thirteen) Vishwadevas, sons of Viswā, मरुतः इति (and forty-nine) Maruts.

 Even after the creation of the Kshatriyas Viraj did not flourish as before in his work for want of somebody to secure wealth for the performance of rites. He created the Vaishyas



having as their deities those classes of gods who abound in groups: The group of eight Vasus, the group of eleven Rudras, the group of twelve Ādityas, the group of thirty-nine Viswadevas, and the seven groups of forty-nine Maruts.

——————————————————————————————
