\[NOTES—1. For they succeed in acquiring wealth mostly in combination, not singly.\]

——————————————————————————————

** स नैव व्यभवत्स शौद्रं वर्णमसृजत पूषणमियं वै। पूषेयꣳ हीदꣳ सर्वं पुष्यति यदिदं किञ्च॥१३॥**

 सः He (Viraj) एव yet, still न not व्यभवत् increased, prospered. सः He असृजत् created शौद्रम् Shudra वर्णम् caste पूषणम् Pushan, nourisher. वै Verily इयम् this (earth) पूषा (is) Pushan; हि Because इयम् this (earth) पुष्यति nourishes सर्वम् all इदम् this यत् किं च whichever इदम् this.

 Even after the creation of the Vaishyas Viraj did not prosper for want of servant. He created the Shudra caste presided over by Pushan (nourisher). This world indeed is Pushan; for it nourishes all that exists.

——————————————————————————————

\[NOTES—1. Pushan is also the deity of the earth.\]

——————————————————————————————

** स नैव व्यभवत्तच्छ्रेयोरूपमत्यसृजत धर्मं तदेतत्क्षत्त्रस्य क्षत्त्रं यद्धर्मस्तस्माद्धर्मात्परं नास्त्यथो अबलीयान्बलीयाꣳसमाशꣳ सते धर्मेण यथा राज्ञैवं यो वै स धर्मः सत्यं वै तत्तस्मात्सत्यं**



**वदन्तमाहुर्धर्मं वदतीति धर्मं वा वदन्तꣳ सत्यं वदतीत्येतद्ध्येवैतदुभयं भवति॥१४॥**

 सः He (Viraj) न not व्यभवत् increased, flourished एव yet, even now, अत्यसृजत् (he) created that श्रेयः good, excellent रुपम् form धर्मम् justice. तत् That एतत् this यत् (=यः) which (is) धर्मः justice, rightness क्षत्रम् Master, controller क्षत्रस्य of the Kshatriya. तस्मात् Than that धर्मात् justice अस्ति is न not (anything) परम् greater, higher. अथः So अबलीयान् the non-strong, weak person आशंसते hopes (to defeat) बलीयांसम् a stronger person धर्मेण by justice यथा as राज्ञा through king. एवम् Thus यः which वै (is) in reality सः that धर्म्मः justice वै (is) verily तत् that सत्यम् truth. तस्मात् Therefore आहुः (the bystanders) say वदन्तम् one speaking सत्यम् the truth, वदति speaks धर्मम् इति what is just, वा or वदन्तम् one speaking धर्मम् what is right वदति speaks सत्यम् इति the truth हि because उभयम् both एतद् these एव indeed भवति is, are एतत् this (rightness).

 Even after the creation of the four castes Viraj was not prosperous enough for he was afraid that the Kshatriya might be fierce. He created that good form called rightness. This rightness is the master of even the Kshatriyas. Therefore there is nothing greater than rightness. That controls all. So even a weak person wishes to conquer another stronger than himself by the power of rightness as in life a householder does



through a king, the most powerful of all. What is rightness is in reality truth. Since it is so the bystanders who know the difference between them, say that one speaking in accordance with the scriptures speaks what is conventionally right or conversely also one speaking what is conventionally right speaks according to the scriptures, because both of them are rightness. \[Hence the precondition of practising the particular forms of rightness is to identify oneself with one or other of the four castes : Brāhman, Kshatriya, Vaishya or Sudra.\]

——————————————————————————————

\[NOTES—1. Truth is the theoretical knowledge of a thing according to scriptures. When the same knowledge is put into practice is called rightness.\]

——————————————————————————————

 ** तदेतद्ब्रह्म क्षत्त्रं विट्शूद्रस्तदग्निनैव देवेषु ब्रह्माभवद् ब्राह्मणो मनुष्येषु क्षत्त्रियेण क्षत्रियो वैश्येन वैश्यः शूद्रेण शूद्रस्तस्मादग्नावेव देवेषु लोकमिच्छन्ते ब्राह्मणे मनुष्येष्वेताभ्याꣳ हि रूपाभ्यां ब्रह्माभवत्। अथ यो ह वा अस्माल्लोकात्स्वं लोकमदृष्ट्वा प्रैति स एनमविदितो न भुनक्ति यथा वेदो वाऽननूक्तोऽन्यद्वा कर्माकृतं यदिह वा अप्यनेवंविन्महत्पुण्यं कर्म करोति तद्धास्यान्ततः क्षीयत एवाऽऽत्मानमेव लोकमुपासीत स य आत्मानमेव लोकमुपास्ते न हास्य कर्म क्षीयते। अस्माद्ध्येवाऽऽत्मनो यद्यत्कामयते तत्तत्सृजते॥१५॥**



 तत् That, thus, so. एतत् this (these, four castes) ब्रह्म the Brāhman, क्षत्रम् the Kshatriya, विट् the Vaishya शूद्रः (and) the Sudra. तत् He (Viraj) अभवत् became, ब्रह्म a Brāhman देवेषु among the gods अग्निना through fire, एव only ब्राह्मणः the Brāhman मनुष्येषु among men. क्षत्रियः a Kshatriya, क्षत्रियेण through the (divine) Kshatriya वैश्यः a Vaishya वैश्येन through the (divine) Vaishya, शूद्रः (and) a Sudra शूद्रेण through the (divine) Sudra. तस्मात् Therefore इच्छन्ते (People) desire, wish to attain लोकम् world, place देवेषु among the gods अग्नौ through fire एव alone मनुष्येषु (and) amongmen ब्राह्मणे through the Brāhman, हि because एताभ्याम् by these two रुपाभ्याम् forms (Brāhman and fire) ब्रह्म Brāhman, Viraj अभवत् was, bеcame, mnifested. अथ Then, if यो who ह वै verily प्रेति goes out, departs अस्मात् from this लोकात् world अदृष्ट्वा not seeing, not knowing स्वम् his own लोकम् world (the self) सः he अविदितः unknown न not भुनक्ति protects, saves एनम् him यथा वा as वेदः the Vedas न-अनूक्तः not studied, unread वा or अन्यत् any (secular) कर्म work (such as agriculture) अकृतम् not done अपि ह even यदि वा if न-एवं वित् one not knowing thus करोति does, performs महत् a good number, a great many पुण्यम् meritorious, holy कर्मम् works, rites तत् ह that, those (acts) असत् his (of theignorant man) क्षीयते perishes एव certainly अन्ततः in the end; (after the enjoyments of fruits). उपासीत (one ) should meditate एव only लोकम् upon the world आत्मानम् the Self. सः He यः who उपास्ते worships, meditates एव only लोकम् upon the world आत्मानम् the self अस्य his कर्म works, rites न हि never क्षीयते are exhausted. अस्मात् From this आत्मनः self एव indeed हि certainly सृजते (he)



creates तत् that तत् that यत् which यत् which कामयते (he) desires.

 Thus were created the four castes: the Brāhman, the Kshatriya, the Vaishya and the Shudra. Viraj, the creator of these castes, directly became a Brāhman god in the form of fire and a Brahman man in the human form. He however assumed a changed form in the other castes. For, indirectly he became a Kshatriya god through Indra and other divine Kshatriyas, a Vaishya god through Vasus and divine Vaishyas and a Shudra god through Pushan and the other divine Shudras. Therefore people seek to attain a place among the gods by performing rites connected with fire. Because Viraj directly became Brahmana and fire, the agent and receptacle of rites respectively. If any one goes out of this world without the knowledge of the Supreme Self, the latter being unknown, fails to save him from grief, delusion and fear by the removal of ignorance, as the Vedas unread does not enlighten one on the rites, etc., or any similar work such as agriculture not performed does not bestow its results. Even if a genius who does not possess the knowledge of the self undertakes a good number of meritorious rites such as a horse-sacrifice in the world, those rites of that man ignorant of the Self are bound to perish after the enjoyment of



the fruits like the splendour arising from the fantasy of a dream. One should therefore meditate only upon the Supreme Self. The works of one who meditates only upon Supreme Self never perishes, simply because he has no work. From this Self he certainly creates whatever he desires.

——————————————————————————————

\[NOTES—1. That is why the Brāhmana by their very birth attain the human results for which they need not perform rites depending on fire. But if they want divine results, they have to resort to rites connected with fire. As it is said in the Mahabharat (2. 87 ) : ‘Brahman attains his life's ends by the repetition of the sacred-formula whether he performs any rite or not. Brahman is a friend of all.’

2\. The eternal fact is again stated here. The man ignorant of the Self continuously suffers from the misery of transmigration by the exhaustion of the results attained by his work. That is not the case with the knower of the Supreme Self. As emperor Janak said—“If Mithila is on fire, nothing mine is burnt.” (Mahabharat 12. 176. 56.)\]

——————————————————————————————

 **अथो अयं वा आत्मा सर्वेषां भूतानां लोकः स यज्जुहोति यद्यजते तेन देवानां लोकोऽथ यदनुब्रूते तेन ऋषीणामथ यत्पितृभ्यो निपृणाति यत्प्रजामिच्छते तेन पितॄणामथ यन्मनुष्यान्वासयते यदेभ्योऽशनं ददाति तेन मनुष्याणामथ यत्पशुभ्यस्तृणोदकं विन्दति तेन पशूनां यदस्य गृहेषु श्वापदा वयाꣳस्या पिपीलिकाभ्य उपजीवन्ति तेन तेषां लोको यथा ह वै स्वाय**



**लोकायारिष्टिमिच्छेदेवꣳ हैवंविदे सर्वाणि भूतान्यरिष्टिमिच्छन्ति तद्वा एतद्विदितं मीमाꣳसितम्॥१६॥**

 अथ Now अयम् this आत्मा self (the ignorant house-holder) वै (is) verily लोकः world, principal stay, support सर्वेषाम् of all भूतानाम् beings. यत् what सः he जुहोति makes oblations (in the fire), यत् what यजते (he) sacrifices तेन by that लोकः world, refuge देवानाम् of the gods. अथ Now यत् what अनुब्रूते (he) repeats, what the teacher says, recites तेन by that ऋषीणाम् (support) of the sages. अथ Now यत् what निपृणाति (he) offers cakes, makes offerings पितृभ्यः to the manes, to the fathers यत् that इच्छते tries to obtain, to raise; desires to have प्रजाम् son, offspring, तेन by that पितृणाम् ( support) to the manes. अथ Now यत् that वासयते (he) makes (men) live, gives shelter मनुष्यान् to men, (and) यत् that ददाति gives अशनम् food एभ्यः to them, तेन by that मनुष्याणाम् (support) to men. अथ Now यत् that विन्दति gives तृण-उदकम् fodder and water पशुभ्यः to animals, तेन by that पशूनाम् (support) to animals. यत् That अस्य his गृहेषु houses श्वापदाः beasts वयांस्य birds आपिपीलिकाभ्यः (and) even the ants उपजीवन्ति live and feed तेन by that लोकः world, refuge तेषाम् to them. यथा ह Just as वै verily इच्छेत् (one) wishes अरिष्टिम् absence of misfortune, safety स्वाय to one's own लोकाय of world, of microcosm, of body, एवं ह so सर्वाणि all भूतानि beings इच्छन्ति wish अरिष्टिम् (न-रिष्टिम्) welfare, non-destruction, एवं विदे to him who knows it thus. तत् That एतत् this (five-fold duty) वै Indeed विदितम् known मीमांसितम् discussed, reasoned.



 Now this householder qualified for rites is verily the support to all beings from the gods down to the worms. He becomes a support to the gods by pouring out libations in the fire and performing sacrifices. By reciting the Vedas he acts as a support to the sages. In so far as he makes offerings of cakes, water, etc., to the Manes and raises off-springs, he is a support to the Manes. He becomes a refuge to men by offering accommodation to them in his house as well as food to them and others who do not stay. As he gives fodder and water to animals he becomes their principal stay. And because beasts, birds—and even the worms are fed by the crumbs, the offerings given to them and washings of utensils etc., in his houses, he is their main prop. Just as one verily wishes welfare to his microcosmic form consisting of the body and organs, so do all beings from gods down to worms wish non-destruction to him who knows it as such. Verily this five-fold duty to gods, sages, Manes, men and animals is known from the Shatapatha Brahman (1.7. 2.1-6), in which they have been well discussed and described as five great sacrifices.

 **आत्मैवेदमग्र आसीदेक एव सोऽकामयत जाया मे स्यादथ प्रजायेयाथ वित्तं मे स्यादथ कर्म कुर्वीयेत्येतावान्वै कामो नेच्छ‍ꣳ**



**श्चानातो भूयो विन्देत्तस्मादप्येतर्ह्येकाकी कामयते जाया मे स्यादथ प्रजायेयाथ वित्तं मे स्यादथ कर्म कुर्वीयेति स यावदप्येतेषामेकैकं न प्राप्नोत्यकृत्स्न एव तावन्मन्यते तस्यो कृत्स्नता मन एवास्याऽऽत्मा वाग्जाया प्राणः प्रजा चक्षुर्मानुषं वित्तं चक्षुषा हि तद्विन्दते श्रोत्रं दैवꣳ श्रोत्रेण हि तच्छृणोत्यात्मैवास्य कर्माऽऽत्मना हि कर्म करोति स एष पाङ्क्तो यज्ञः पाङ्क्तः पशुः पाङ्क्तः पुरुषः पाङ्क्तमिदꣳ सर्वं यदिदं किञ्च तदिदं सर्वमाप्नोति य एवं वेद॥१७॥ इति चतुर्थं ब्राह्मणम्॥४॥**

 इदम् This आत्मा self ( ignorant man) आसीत् was अग्रे before (marriage) एव indeed एकः one, single (entity) एव only सः he अकामयत desired इति thus मे to me स्यात् let there be जायां a wife. अथ Next प्रजायेय let (me) have progeny. अथ Next मे (let) me स्यात् have वित्तम् wealth. अथ Next कुर्वीय let (me) perform कर्म work, sacrifices. एतावान् This much वै verily कामः desire. न Not विन्दत् (one) would get, might have भूयः more अतः than this च and न not इच्छन् wishing. तस्मात् Therefore अपि even एतर्हि to this day, now एकाकी (being) single कामयते (one) desires इति thus मे to me स्यात् let. there be जाया a wife. अथ Moreover प्रजायेय let ( me) have offspring. अथ And मे to me स्यात् let there be वित्तम् wealth. अथ Moreover कुर्वीय let (me) perform कर्म work, rites. यावत् As long सः he न not प्राप्नोति gets, obtains अपि even एक-एकम् each one एतेषाम् of these तावत् so long एव only मन्यते (he) thinks, considers (himself) अकृत्स्नः (न-कृत्स्रः) not complete, not whole. तस्य His कृत्स्नता fullness. wholeness,



completeness उ also मनः the mind (is) एव indeed अस्य his आत्मा Self, वाक् speech जाया wife, प्राणः life, vital power, प्रजा progeny, चक्षुः the eye, मानुषम् human वित्तम् wealth. हि Because चक्षुषा by the eye, विन्दते (he) obtains, तत् that, it, (human wealth) the ear, दैवम् divine, belonging to the gods (वित्तम् wealth) हि because श्रोत्रेण by the ear शृणोति (he) hears तत् it, (divine wealth) आत्मा the body एव indeed तस्य his कर्म rite, हि because करोति (he) performs कर्म rites आत्मना by the body. सः That एषः this यज्ञः sacrifice (is) पाङ्क्तः five-folds, having five factors पशुः the animal पाङ्क्तः (has) five-folds, five factors पुरुषः the man पाङ्क्तः (has) five-factors, सर्वम् all इदम् this (means or the ends of rites) यत् इदं किं च that whichever पाङ्क्तम् (has) five-factors यः Who वेद knows, realises एवम् thus (as the five-fold sacrifices) आप्नोति obtains, get तत् that इदम् this सर्वम् all (Universe).

 This man was indeed before marriage single one in existence. He desired thus: Let me have a wife who will make me qualified for the sacrifices so that I may have progeny. And let me have wealth such as cattle, so that I may perform regular and occasional rites that will confer prosperity and liberation on me. Desire indeed extends no further than these objects. One cannot obtain through desire anything more than these things in spite of his wishes. Therefore even now a man being single before marriage desires thus: Let me have a wife, so that I may have offspring,



let me have wealth so that I may perform sacrifices. As long as he does not get all of them—wife, son, wealth—so long he does not think himself whole. The wholeness of this man verily comes in this way. The mind being the chief of the body and organs is like his Self as the head of a family is as it were the Self of the wife and others. Speech is like his wife, for speech follows the mind as the wife does her husband: Vital power is his progeny, for it is created by mind and speech for performing sacrifices: The eye is his human wealth because it sees cows, etc., that are used in the sacrifices: The ear is his divine wealth, because meditation concerning gods depends on it and the body is the rite because he performs rites by it. This sacrifice is therefore five-fold and is performed even without rites. The animals such as cows are five-fold and the men are five-fold. In short, the means and the ends of rites whatsoever are five-fold. He who realises himself to be the five-fold sacrifice attains all this universe as his own Self.

——————————————————————————————

\[NOTES 1. A natural ignorant man of the upper three castes identified with the microcosm consisting of the body and organs.

2\. The self-same desire assume two-fold aspects of means and ends. An ignorant man goaded by desire helplessly

——————————————————————————————



——————————————————————————————

gets enmeshed in it like the silk-worm in the cocoon and forgets his real self. As Taittiriya Brahmana ( 3.10.11. 1.) observes: They are ignorant of their true self, as they are attached to the sacrifices, do them with fire and get choked by their smoke.

3\. Life can be summed up in these two hankerings: means and ends—either visible or invisible that can be acquired. Desire consists of only these two hankerings after means and ends.

4\. Speech here means words conveying injunction and prohibition which the mind receives through the ear, understands and uses.\]

——————————————————————————————

**CHAPTER ONE: SECTION FIVE**

 **यत्सप्तान्नानि मेधया तपसाऽजनयत्पिता। एकमस्य साधारणं द्वे देवानभाजयत्। त्रीण्यात्मनेऽकुरुत पशुभ्य एकं प्रायच्छत्। तस्मिन्सर्वं प्रतिष्ठितं यच्च प्राणिति यच्च न। कस्मात्तानि न क्षीयन्तेऽद्यमानानि सर्वदा यो वैतामक्षितिं वेद सोऽन्नमत्ति प्रतीकेन। स देवानपिगच्छति स ऊर्जमुपजीवतीति श्लोकाः॥१॥**

 यत् When, which पिता the father (of creation), creator अजनयत् created, produced सप्त seven (kinds of) अन्नानि food, object of enjoyment मेधया by knowledge, by meditation तपसा (and) by penance, by rites (I will disclose). एकम् One अस्य of this (world) साधारणम् (is) common, general. द्वे Two अभाजयत् (he) assigned, apportioned देवान् to the gods. त्रीणि



Three अकुरुत (he) made, kept आत्मने for himself. एकम् one प्रायच्छत् (he) gave, allotted, पशुभ्यः to the animals. तस्मिन् In it सर्वम् all (this world) प्रतिष्ठितम् rests, is dependent यत् च whatever प्रणिति breaths, lives च and यत् whatever न not (breathes, lives) कस्मात् why तानि they न not क्षीयन्ते are exhausted अद्यमानानि being eaten, being consumed सर्वदा constantly, always. सः He यः who वै indeed वेद knows ताम् that अक्षितिम् inexhaustible, imperishable अत्ति eats, enjoys अन्नम् food, object of enjoyment प्रतीकेन without effort. सः He अपि even गच्छति goes देवान् to the gods. सः He उपजीवति lives on ऊर्जम् food, that gods eat, nectar इति thus श्लोकाः (are) The Verses, the Mantras.

 When the creator created seven kinds of food by knowledge (meditation) and penance (rites), one of them was the general food of all beings. Two he assigned to the gods. Three he kept for himself and one he allotted to the animals. Whatever breathes and whatever breathes not are all dependent on them. Why are the foods not exhausted though they are being constantly consumed? He who knows them as inexhaustible eats food without effort. He goes to the gods and lives on the food of the gods. These are the Mantras.

——————————————————————————————

\[NOTES 1. Here creator not only means Hiranyagarbha but every being in a certain creation who performs knowledge (meditation) and penance (rites) according to the scriptures. For like Hiranyagarbha every being becomes the

——————————————————————————————



father of all in the next creation as every one is both the enjoyer and the object of enjoyment of the whole Universe—Anandagiri.\]

 **यत्सप्तान्नानि मेधया तपसाऽजनयत्पितेति मेधया हि तपसाऽजनयत्पिता। एकमस्य साधारणमितीदमेवास्य तत्साधारणमन्नं यदिदमद्यते। स य एतदुपास्ते न स पाप्मनो व्यावर्तत मिश्रꣳ ह्येतत्। द्वे देवानभाजयदिति हतं च प्रहतं च तस्माद्देवेभ्यो जुह्वति च प्र च जुह्वत्यथो आहुर्दर्शपूर्णमासाविति। तस्मान्नेष्टियाजुकः स्यात्। पशुभ्य एकं प्रायच्छदिति तत्पयः। पयो ह्येवाग्रे मनुष्याश्च पशवश्चोपजीवन्ति तस्मात्कुमारं जातं घृतं वैवाग्रे प्रतिलेहयन्ति स्तनं वाऽनुधापयन्त्यथ वत्सं जातमाहुरतृणाद इति। तस्मिन्सर्वं प्रतिष्ठितं यच्च प्राणिति यच्च नेति पयसि हीदꣳ सर्वं प्रतिष्ठितं यच्च प्राणिति यच्च न तद्यदिदमाहुः संवत्सरं पयसा जुह्वदप पुनर्मृत्युं जयतीति न तथा विद्याद्यदहरेव जुहोति तदहः पुनर्मृत्युमप जयत्येवं विद्वान्सर्वं हि देवेभ्योऽन्नाद्यं प्रयच्छति। कस्मात्तानि न क्षीयन्तेऽद्यमानानि सर्वदेति पुरुषो वा अक्षितिः स हीदमन्नं पुनः पुनर्जनयते। यो वैतामक्षितिं वेदेति पुरुषो वा अक्षितिः स हीदमन्नं धिया धिया जनयते कर्मभिर्यद्धैतन्न कुर्यात्क्षीयेत ह सोऽन्नमत्ति प्रतीकेनेति मुखं प्रतीकं मुखेनेत्येतत्। स देवानपिगच्छति स ऊर्जमुपजीवतीति प्रशꣳसा॥२॥**

 यत् That, when पिता father, creator, अजनयत् created, produced सप्त अन्नानि seven kinds of food मेधया by intelligence,



तपसा by meditation, by penance, by rites-इति (means) thus—पिता father, creator, हि verily अजनयत् created (them) मेधया by intelligence, by knowledge तपसा by austerity, by rites एकम् one (food) अस्य of this (world) साधारणम् (is) general, common इति (means) thus; इदम् This (food) एव indeed यत् which इदम् this अद्यते is eaten तत् that (is) साधारणम् common अन्नम् food. सः He यः who उपास्ते adores, is devoted to this सः he न never व्यावर्त्तते turns, is free पाप्मनः from sins, from evils, हि for एतत् thus (is) मिश्रम् general (food). द्वे Two अभाजयत् (he) distributed, apportioned देवान् to the gods इति (means) thus हुतं च oblations poured in the fire प्रहुतं च and offerings made to the gods. तस्मात् Therefore जुह्वति च (they) pour oblations च and प्रजुह्वति make offsprings देवेभ्यः to the gods. अथ उ
However, on the otherhand, आहुः (some) say, hold—दर्श-पूर्णमासौ इति sacrifices at the new moon and full moon. तस्मात् Therefore न not स्यात् (one ) should be \*इष्टि-याजुकः sacrificer for secular results. एकम् One प्रायच्छत् (he) gave पशुभ्यः इति to the animals. तत् That (is) पयः milk, हि for अग्रे first, infancy मनुष्याः च men च and पशवः animals उपजीवन्ति live on एव only पयः milk. तस्मात् Therefore वै verily अग्रे first प्रतिलेहयन्ति (men) make lick जातम् new born कुमारम् babe, child घृतं वा melted butter, वा or अनुधापयन्ति make suck स्तनम् breast. अथ And आहुः (they) say जातम् new-born वत्सम् calf अतृणादः इति non-eater of grass, तस्मिन् on it (milk) सर्वम् all प्रतिष्ठितम् rests, depends यत् च which प्राणिति breaths lives च and यत् इति which न does not, हि for इदम् this सर्वम् all प्रतिष्ठितम् depends, rests

——————————————————————————————

\* ‘Ishti’ hear means ‘Kamyeshti’=sacrifice with secular results This is known from the Shatapatha Brahmana (1.3. 5.10.)

——————————————————————————————



पयसि on milk यत् इदम् this आहुः (some Brāhmans) say यत् that संवत्सरम् the whole year पयसा with milk जुह्वत making offerings अपजयति conquers पुनर्मृत्युम् इति repeated death. न Not विद्यात् (one) should know, understood तथा in that sense. एवम् Such विद्वान् knower अपजयति conquers पुनर्मृत्युम् further death तत् that अहः day यत् अहः on which day एव indeed जुहति makes offering हि for प्रयच्छति gives अन्न-आद्यम् eatable food, देवेभ्यः to the gods. कस्मात् why तानि these (foods) न not क्षीयन्ते are finished, are exhausted अद्यमानानि being eaten, being consumed सर्वदा इति always, constantly पुरुषः the being वै verily अक्षितिः (is their) permanence, inexhaustibility हि for सः he जनयते creates इदम् this अन्नम् food पुनः again पुनः and again यः वा who वेद knows एताम् these अक्षितिम् इति permanent, inexhaustible पुरुषः eater वै indeed अक्षितिम् (is) the (cause of their) inexhaustibility हि for, in fact सः he जनयते creates इदम् this अन्नम् food धिया by intelligence, by meditation धिया by intelligence, by meditation कर्मभिः (and) rites; यत् ह if, when न not कुर्यात् (he) should do एतत् this ह indeed क्षीयते (it) is exhausted, सः he अत्ति eats अन्नम् food प्रतीकेन इति by Pratik. प्रतीकम् Pratik मुखम् (is) face, eminence, effortlessness एतत् this (means) मुखेन इति by face, by eminence, effortlessness. सः he अपिगच्छति goes to, attains देवान् the gods. सः He उपजीवति lives on ऊर्जम् food of the gods, nectar—इति this प्रशंसा eulogy, praise.

 When it is said that the creator created seven kinds of food through knowledge and penance, it is clear that the creator verily created them through knowledge and penance. The Mantra ‘one is the



general food to all beings’ means that this food which is eaten daily by all eaters is general to all eaters. He who is devoted to this general food to prolong his life instead of performing sacrifices is never removed from sins; because this food is the common property of all. The Mantra ‘Two he distributed to the gods’ means the two foods in the form of oblations poured in the fire and other offerings made to the gods. Therefore householders even now offer food to the gods by making oblations in the fire and then giving them other presents. Some hold that the new-moon and full-moon sacrifices are meant by these two kinds of food and not the above two offerings. In order to keep them intact for the gods, one should not be occupied with rites for secular results. The food that the creator gave to the animals is milk. Because men and animals live on milk only during infancy, therefore men make a new-born child lick melted butter in contact with gold in the post-natal ceremony or make it suck the breast. And the animals only suckle the young one; so they say that a new-born calf is a non-eater of grass. The meaning of the Mantra ‘on it depends all that breathes and that breathes not’ is that the whole animate and inanimate world rests on milk. It is said in some Brahmanas that by making offering



of milk in the fire for a year one overcomes repeated death. The Mantras should not be understood in that sense. He who knows as described above overcomes repeated death on that very day in which he makes that offering. Because he dedicates all eatable food to the gods by means of morning and evening oblations. The Mantra ‘Why are they not finished though they are continuously being consumed’—means that the eater is verily the cause of their inexhaustibility because he creates all this food, again and again by knowledge and penance. The Mantra ‘He who knows these foods inexhaustible’ means that the eater is in fact the cause of their inexhaustibility, because he creates this food repeatedly by knowledge and rites (that is, by the efforts of his speech, mind and body). When he stops doing this for a moment the food will be finished. He eats food with Pratika: Pratika means face, eminence. Hence the meaning of the Mantra is that he enjoys food with eminence and gets identified with the gods. He lives on nectar—is an eulogistic statement.

——————————————————————————————

\[NOTES—1. Similar view is expressed in the following sacred texts. Rig Veda (10. 117. 6.) says: ‘The food that an ignorant person eats without offering to the gods brings death to him.’ Mahabharat (12. 246. 5.) says: ‘One must

——————————————————————————————



——————————————————————————————

not cook food only for oneself.’ Gita (3.12.) says: ‘He who eats food without giving to the gods is a thief.’ Manu Samhita (8.317.) says: ‘The destroyer of a foetus can throw his sin in one who eats food without setting apart for others.’ Taittiriya Upanishad says (3.10. 6): ‘I devour that man (as food) who eats without giving to others.

2\. According to these Brahmanas three hundred and sixty oblations are offered in one year taking morning and evening oblations as one. The bricks by which the altar for the Agnihotra sacrifice is built are called Yajusmati and have the same number. The oblations are imagined as these bricks and so also are the days of the year.’

3\. After death he becomes identified with the Universe and does not take another birth to make further death possible.

4\. He has not to await the result for a year but attains in a single day the same which is identity with the Universe.

5\. As it is said in Shatapatha Brahmana (13. 7. 1. 1) thus: ‘One desiring union with Hiranyagarbha performed sacrifices. He thoug—as sacrifices never produce eternal results let me offer myself in all beings and all beings in me’. By offering himself in all beings and all beings in himself he attained highest place among all beings as well as identity with all the gods.

6\. Therefore the whole Universe is a series of actions and results, means and ends. It is unreal and flimsy like flowing stream or a burning lamp. As a banana stalk is without fibre, so it is devoid of substance or reality. It is as illusory as a foam, mirage or a dream. But this unreal Universe appears real and eternal to them who identify themselves with it. The Upanishad inculcates the knowledge of Brahman only for those who are disgusted with the Universe and desires to get rid of it.

——————————————————————————————



——————————————————————————————

7\. He eats food and never becomes the food. Unlike an ignorant man he is the self of the foods, and is only their eater but never the food.\]

——————————————————————————————

 ** त्रीण्यात्मनेऽकुरुतेति मनो वाचं प्राणं तान्यात्मनेऽकुरुतान्यत्रमना अभूवं नादर्शमन्यत्रमना अभूवं नाश्रौषमिति मनसा ह्येव पश्यति मनसा शृणोति। कामः सङ्कल्पो विचिकित्सा श्रद्धाऽश्रद्धा धृतिरधृतिर्ह्रीर्धीर्भीरित्येतत्सर्वं मन एव तस्मादपि पृष्ठत उपस्पृष्टो मनसा विजानाति यः कश्च शब्दो वागेव सा। एषा ह्यन्तमायत्तैषा हि न प्राणोऽपानो व्यान उदानः समानोऽन इत्येतत्सर्वं प्राण एवैतन्मयो वा अयमात्मा वाङ्मयो मनोमयः प्राणमयः॥३॥**

 त्रीणि Three (kinds of food) आत्मने for himself अकुरुत इति (he) made, disigned—मनः the mind वाचम् the speech प्राणम् the vital power; तानि these आत्मने for himself अकुरुत (he) made, designed (People say ) इति Thus अन्यत्र-मना absent-minded, unmindful अभूवम् (I) was, न not अदर्शम् (I) saw, अन्यत्र-मना absent-minded अभूवम् (I) was न not अश्रौषम् (I) heard; हि because मनसा by the mind एव only पश्यति (one) sees, मनसा by the mind शृणोति (one) hears. कामः Desire सङ्कल्पः deliberation विचिकित्सा doubt, श्रद्धा faith, अश्रद्धा want of faith, धृति steadiness, patience, अधृति want of steadiness, impatience, ह्रीः modesty, shame, धीः intelligence भीः इति fear—सर्वम् all एतत् this (are) एव indeed, मनः the mind. तस्मात् Therefore अपि even उपस्पृष्टः (one) being touched पृष्ठतः



on the back, from behind विजानाति knows मनसा by the mind एव alone यः that कः च whatever शब्दः sound (is), सा that (is) एव indeed वाक् speech; हि because एषा it आयत्ता traces, determines अन्तम् end (of everything). एषा It (is) हि indeed नः not (revealed ) प्राणः Prāna, अपानः Apana व्यानः Vyāna, उदानः Udana, समानः Samāna, अनः इति Ana सर्वम् all एतत् this (are) एवं but प्राणः Prāna. अयम् This आत्मा self, microcosm वै verily एतत्-मयः full of these, composed of these, वाक्-मयः full of speech, मनोमयः full of mind प्राणमयः (and) full of life, vital power.

 Prajapati, the father of creation, made for himself three kinds of food. It means that the father assigned for himself the mind, speech and the vital power. They say, I did not see the object as my mind was elsewhere; I did not hear this because my mind was engaged elsewhere. Every body sees and hears through the mind. Desire, deliberation, doubt, faith, want of faith, steadiness, impatience, shame, intelligence and fear—all these are nothing but the forms of mind. Because even if one is touched on the back invisibly by any body, one knows it distinctly by the mind whether it is a touch of the hand or knee. Therefore the internal organ called mind does exist. All kinds of sound in the world-whether it be an articulate sound of a creature or an inarticulate sound of the musical instrument or clouds—



are nothing but speech; because being luminous like a lamp it reveals other objects but it cannot itself be revealed by others like objects. Prāna, Apāna, Samana, Vyana, Udana and Ana are only particular functions of the vital power. This microcosm called the Self is composed of these three. It is composed of the speech, the mind and the vital power of Hiranyagarbha.

——————————————————————————————

\[NOTES—1. Mind is the internal organ that joins itself with form, sound and other sense-objects to make perception possible. Perception is impossible in its absence. Even if the external organ is connected with the respective object one does not perceive the object without the presence and cooperation of the mind. It also helps to distinguish between perceptions.

2\. Sexual attraction, etc.

3\. Consideration of a thing lying in front of us whether it is white or blue and so on.

4\. Belief in the efficacy of sacrifices to produce results in the hereafter; also belief in the existence of the gods, etc.

5\. Prana is the nerve function connected with the heart. It can move to the mouth and the nostrils. It is called Prana as it issues in front.

6\. Apana functions below the heart and extends up to the navel; it is called Apana as it helps excretion.

7\. Vyana regulates the Prān and Apān and is the nexus between the two. It is also the cause of actions that require strength.

——————————————————————————————



——————————————————————————————

8\. Samana is so called as it can assimilate what we eat and drink. It is seated in the belly and helps the digestion of food.

9\. Udana causes nutrition, rising up, etc. It permeates the whole body from the sole of the feet to the head and functions upwards.

10\. Ana is the general nerve function concerned with the activities of the body.\]

——————————————————————————————

 ** त्रयो लोका एत एव वागेवायं लोको मनोऽन्तरिक्षलोकः प्राणोऽसौ लोकः॥४॥**

 एते These एव indeed (are) त्रयः three लोकाः worlds. वाक् speech (is) एव verily अयम् this लोकः world, earth. मनः The mind (is) अन्तरिक्ष-लोकः sky. प्राणः Vital power (is) असौ that लोकः world (heaven).

 These are indeed the three worlds: Speech is indeed the earth, the mind is the sky and the vital power is the heaven.

** त्रयो वेदा एत एव वागेवर्ग्वेदो मनो यजुर्वेदः प्राणः सामवेदः॥५॥ **

 एते These एव indeed त्रयः (are) three वेदाः Vedas वाक् speech एव indeed; ऋक्-वेदः (is) the Rik-Veda मनः the mind (is) यजुः-वेद the Yajur-Veda (and) प्राणः the Vital Power, life force साम-वेदः the Sāma-Veda.



 These are indeed three Vedas: Speech is indeed the Rig-Veda, the mind is the Yajur-Veda and the vital power is the Sāma-Veda.

 **देवाः पितरो मनुष्या एत एव वागेव देवा मनः पितरः प्राणो मनुष्याः॥६॥**

 एते These एव indeed देवाः (are) the gods, पितरः the manes, मनुष्याः (and) the men, वाक् speech (is) एव indeed देवाः the gods, मनः the mind (is) the पितरः the manes (and) मनुष्याः men (are) प्राणः the life force.

 These are indeed the gods, the Manes and men. Speech is indeed the gods, the mind is the Manes and vital power is men.

 **पिता माता प्रजैत एव मन एव पिता वाङ्माता प्राणः प्रजा॥७॥**

 एते These एव indeed (are) पिता the father, माता the mother (and) प्रजा the child, मनः the mind (is) एव indeed पिता the father वाक् speech (is) माता the mother, (and) प्राणः the Vital Power (is) प्रजा the child.

 These are indeed the father, mother and child. The mind is indeed the father, speech is the mother and the vital power is the child.

 **विज्ञातं विजिज्ञास्यमविज्ञातमेव एव यत्किञ्च विज्ञातं वाचस्तद्रूपं वाग्घि विज्ञाता वागेनं तद्भूत्वाऽवति॥८॥**



 एते These एव indeed (are) विज्ञातम् the known, विजिज्ञास्यम् what is to be known, (and) अविज्ञातम् the unknown. यत् किं च whatever (is) विज्ञातम् known वाचः speech तत्-रुपम् (is) of that form, हि because वाक् speech (is) विज्ञाता the knower वाक् the speech अवति protects, preserves, एनम् him भूत्वा by becoming तत् that.

 These are indeed what is known, what is to be known and what is unknown. Speech assumes the form of whatever is clearly known; because speech is the knower. Speech protects him who knows its particular manifestations (as given above) by becoming what is known.

——————————————————————————————

\[NOTES—1. Speech being self-luminous brings other objects to light.

2\. By becoming the object of his enjoyment in that form.\]

——————————————————————————————

 **यत्किञ्च विजिज्ञास्यं मनसस्तद्रूपं मनो हि विजिज्ञास्यं मन एनं तद्भूत्वाऽवति॥९॥**

 यत् किं च whatever (is) विजिज्ञास्यम् to be known तत्-रुपम् that form मनसः (is) of the mind, हि because मनः the mind (is) विजिज्ञास्यम् what is to be known, मनः the mind अवति protects एनम् him भूत्वा by becoming तत् that.

 The mind assumes the form of whatever is clearly to be known. Since the mind considers the pros and cons of a thing it is what is to be



known. The mind protects him who knows its manifestations by becoming what is to be known.

——————————————————————————————

\[NOTES—1. The object of his enjoyment in that form.\]

——————————————————————————————

 **यत्किञ्चाविज्ञातं प्राणस्य तद्रूपं प्राणो ह्यविज्ञातः प्राण एनं तद्भूत्वाऽवति॥१०॥**

 यत् किं च Whatever (is) अविज्ञातम् unknown तत्-रुपम् that form (is) प्राणस्य of the Vital power, हि because प्राणः the Vital power (is) अविज्ञातः what is unknown. प्राणः the Vital power अवति supports एनम् him भूत्वा by becoming तत् that.

 The vital power takes the form of whatever is completely unknown (and not even suspected), because vital power is what is unknown. The vital power protects him who knows its manifestations by becoming his food in the form of what is unknown.

 **तस्यै वाचः पृथिवी शरीरं ज्योतीरूपमयमग्निस्तद्यावत्येव वाक्तावती पृथिवी तावानयमग्निः॥११॥**

 तस्यौ (=तस्या) वाचः of that speech पृथिवी the earth (is) शरीरम् the body, the non-luminous container. अयम् This अग्निः (earthly) fire (is) ज्योतिः-रुपम् the luminous form (the content) तत् so यावती एव as far as वाक् speech (extends), तावती so far पृथिवी the earth तावान् so far अयम् this अग्निः (earthly) fire.



 The earth is the non-luminous container of that speech and the earthly fire is its luminous content. And as far as speech in its two-fold aspect extends, so far extends the earth and so far does this fire.

 **अथैतस्य मनसो द्यौः शरीरं ज्योतीरूपमसावादित्यस्तद्यावदेव मनस्तावती द्यौस्तावानसावादित्यस्तौ मिथुन‍ꣳसमैतां ततः प्राणोऽजायत स इन्द्रः स एषोऽसपत्नो द्वितीयो वै सपत्नो नास्य सपत्नो भवति य एवं वेद॥१२॥ **

 अथ Next द्यौः heaven शरीरम् (is) the body, the container एतस्य of this मनसः mind, असौ that आदित्यः Sun ज्योतिः-रुपम् (is its) luminous form (content). तत् Therefore यावत् एव as far as मनः the mind (spreads), तावती so far द्यौः heaven, तावान् so far असौ this आदित्यः sun तौ the two (fire and sun) समैताम् got, came मिथुनम् into union. ततः From that (union) प्राणः the vital power अजायत was born. सः It (is) इन्द्रः Indra, the lord. सः It एषः this न-सपत्नः (is) without a rival, द्वितीयः a second (being) वै indeed (is) सपत्नः a rival, an adversary यः who वेद knows एवम् as such अस्य his सपत्नः rival, adversary न not भवति exists.

 Heaven is the container of this mind and this seen is its luminous content. Therefore as far as the mind in its two-fold aspect spreads so far spreads heaven and so far does this seen. Fire



(a form of speech) and the seen (a form of the mind) resolving to do the functions of the father and the mother respectively were united between heaven and earth. And from that union the vital power symbolised by air was born and function as vibration. Vital power is the Lord. It is without an adversary. A second being is indeed an adversary. No adversary exists for him who knows the vital power as having no adversary.

 ** अथैतस्य प्राणस्याऽऽपः शरीरं ज्योतीरूपमसौ चन्द्रस्तद्यावानेव प्राणस्तावत्य आपस्तावानसौ चन्द्रस्त एते सर्व एव समाः सर्वेऽनन्ताः स यो हैतानन्तवत उपास्तेऽन्तवन्तꣳस लोकं जयत्यथ यो हैताननन्तानुपास्तेऽनन्तरꣳ स लोकं जयति॥१३॥**

 अथ Now, next आपः water शरीरम् (is) the body, the container. एतस्य Of this प्राणस्य vital power, असौ this चन्द्रः moon ज्योतिः-रुपम् (is) the light-form, luminous content. तत् So, therefore यावान् as far as एव indeed प्राणः the vital power तावान् so far असौ this चन्द्रः moon. ते Those एते these एव indeed सर्वे all (three) समाः (are) equal; alike सर्वे all (three) अनन्ताः (are) infinite, endless. सः He यः who उपास्ते worships, meditates upon ह indeed एतान् these अन्तवतः limited, finite, सः he जयति conquers, wins अन्तवन्तम् finite, limited लोकम् world. अथ But, on the other hand सः he यः who उपास्ते worships, meditates upon एतान् these (three) infinite, as unlimited, जयति conquers, wins अनन्तम् unlimited infinite लोकम् world.



 Water is the container of this vital power that is the food of Hiranyagarbha. This moon is its luminous content (organ). And as far as the vital power in its aspects of the body and organs extends, so far extends water and so far does this moon. These three kinds of food are all equally extensive and are all endless. Whoever worships these three as limited conquers a limited world. On the other hand, whoever worships these as unlimited conquers an unlimited world.

——————————————————————————————

\[NOTES—1. Speech, mind and the vital power created by Hiranyagarbha, the father. These three pervade the whole universe in its aspects of the body and the elements. There is nothing besides them, as Hiranyagarbha is the seen of these all.

2\. They pervade whatever concerns the animate world in its aspects of the body and the elements.

3\. Last as long as the relative Universe which consists of only the bodies and organs.

4\. Born as finite, not identified with these.

5\. Consisting of the whole Universe, a part and parcel of all beings.\]

——————————————————————————————

 **स एष संवत्सरः प्रजापतिः षोडशकलस्तस्य रात्रय एव पञ्चदश कला ध्रुवैवास्य षोडशी कला स रात्रिभिरेवाऽऽ च पूर्यतेऽप च क्षीयते सोऽमावास्याꣳ रात्रिमेतया षोडश्या कलया सर्वमिदं प्राणभृदनुप्रविश्य ततः प्रातर्जायते तस्मादेताꣳ रात्रिं**



**प्राणभृतः प्राणं न विच्छिन्द्यादपि कृकलासस्यैतस्या एव देवताया अपचित्यै॥१४॥**

 सः He एषः this प्रजापतिः Prajapati, Hiranyagarbha (consisting of the kinds of food) षोडशकलः sixteen members (digits) संवत्सरः (is) the full year, time तस्य his रात्रयः nights (and the days) the lunar days पञ्चदशः (are) the fifteen कलाः parts, digits. अस्य His षोड़शी sixteenth कला member, digit एव (is) verily ध्रुवः fixed, constant. सः He आ-पूर्यते च becomes full, waxes रात्रिभिः by the nights (and days) the lunar days एव certainly च as well as अपक्षीयते is wasted, wanes. सः Prajapati अमावस्याम् on the new moon रात्रिम् night एतया by this षोड़श्या sixteenth कलया part अनुप्रविश्य entering, pervading सर्वम् all इदम् this प्राणभृत् living beings. ततः Then जायते is born, joined (to the second member) प्रातः the (following) morning. तस्मात् Therefore एताम् on this रात्रिम् (new moon) night प्राणम् the life प्राणभृतः of living beings न not विच्छिन्द्यात् should cut off, should be killed अपि even कृकलासस्य of a lizard, of a chameleon, अपचित्यै in adoration, in honour एव even एतस्याः of this देवतायाः diety (moon).

 This Prajāpati consisting of the three kinds of food has sixteen members and is Time. The lunar days are his fifteen members and his sixteenth member is fixed. As the moon Prajapati waxes as well as wanes by the lunar days. Through the fixed sixteenth member Prajapati who is Time pervades all the living beings by means of the



water they drink—and the herbs they eat on the new moon night and staying there overnight is joined to the second member. Therefore on the new moon night one should not kill the living beings, not even a lizard, even in honour of moon.

 ** यो वै स संवत्सरः प्रजापतिः षोडशकलोऽयमेव स योऽयमेवंवित्पुरुषस्तस्य वित्तमेव पञ्चदश कला आत्मैवास्य षोडशी कला स वित्तेनैवाऽऽच पूर्यतेऽप च क्षीयते तदेतन्नाभ्यं यदयमात्मा प्रधिर्वित्तं तस्माद्यद्यपि सर्वज्यानिं जीयत आत्मना चेज्जीवति प्रधिनाऽगादित्येवाऽऽहुः॥१५॥**

 सः He यः who वै (is) verily प्रजापतिः Prajapati, Hiranyagarbha षोड़शकलः of sixteen members संवत्सरः (is) the full year, time. अयम् (is) this एव verily सः he यः who अयम् this पुरुषः the person, the sage, एवंवित् who knows thus तस्य his वित्तम् wealth एव indeed पञ्चदशः fifteen members. तस्य His आत्मा the body एव verily षोड़शी sixteenth कला member. सः He आ-पूर्यते च increases, attains fullness च and अपक्षीयते decreases वित्तेन by wealth एव indeed. तत् That एतत् this नाभ्यम् nave of a wheel यत् which अयम् (is) this आत्मा body प्रधिः the periphery, the external outfit, वित्तम् (is) wealth. तस्मात् Therefore यदि if अपि even जीयते is lost सर्व-ज्यानिम् all the wealth, चेत् if आत्मना by himself जीवति he lives, is alive आहुः (people) say इति thus अगात् is gone प्रधिना by the periphery, by the external outfit एव only.



 That Prajapati who consists of sixteen members and is Time is verily the sage who knows the former as identical with himself. Wealth such as cattle is his fifteen members and the body is his sixteenth member corresponding to the fixed member of the moon. Like the moon he increases and decreases by wealth. This body is fit to be the nave and wealth, the external outfit like spokes and the felloes of a wheel. Therefore even if all wealth of a man is lost but he himself remains alive, people say that his external outfit only is gone (like a wheel losing its spokes and felloes except the nave).

——————————————————————————————

\[NOTES —1. Because when he lives, he can again grow by means of wealth.\]

——————————————————————————————

** अथ त्रयो वाव लोका मनुष्यलोकः पितृलोको देवलोक इति सोऽयं मनुष्यलोकः पुत्रेणैव जय्यो नान्येन कर्मणा कर्मणा पितृलोको विद्यया देवलोको देवलोको वै लोकानाꣳ श्रेष्ठस्तस्माद्विद्यां प्रशसन्ति॥१६॥**

 अथ Now वाव verily (there are) त्रयः three लोकाः worlds—मनुष्य-लोकः world of men, पितृ-लोकः world of the fathers (the manes) देव-लोकः इति world of gods. सः That अयम् this मनुष्य-लोकः world of men जय्यः is attainable एव indeed पुत्रेण by the son न not अन्येन by other कर्मणा rites (nor even meditation); पितृ-लोकः world of the fathers कर्मणा by



rites (such as Agnihotra) देव-लोकः world of gods विद्यया by knowledge, by meditation, देव-लोकः the world of gods (is) वै verily श्रेष्ठः (is) best, highest लोकानाम् of this (three) worlds. तस्मात् Therefore प्रशंसन्ति (they) praise विद्याम् knowledge, meditation.

 There are verily three worlds—the world of men, the world of the fathers and the world of the gods. This world of men is attainable only through the means of son, not by rite nor meditation. The world of manes is gained only through rites (such as Agnihotra) not by any other means. Similarly the world of the gods is won only through knowledge (meditation). The world of the gods is the highest of the three worlds. Therefore they praise knowledge (meditation) as the means of its attainment.

 **अथातः सम्प्रत्तिर्यदा प्रैष्यन्मन्यतेऽथ पुत्रमाह त्वं ब्रह्म त्वं यज्ञस्त्वं लोक इति स पुत्रः प्रत्याहाहं ब्रह्माहं यज्ञोऽहं लोक इति यद्वै किञ्चानूक्तं तस्य सर्वस्य ब्रह्मेत्येकता। ये वै के च यज्ञास्तेषा‍ꣳ सर्वेषां यज्ञ इत्येकता ये वै के च लोकास्तेषाꣳ सर्वेषां लोक इत्येकतैतावद्वा इदꣳ सर्वमेतन्मा सर्व‍ꣳ सन्नयमितोऽभुनजदिति तस्मात्पुत्रमनुशिष्टं लोक्यमाहुस्तस्मादेनमनुशासति स यदैवंविदस्माल्लोकात्प्रैत्यथैभिरेव प्राणैः सह पुत्रमाविशति। स यद्यनेन किञ्चिदक्ष्णयाऽकृतं भवति तस्मादेनꣳ सर्वस्मात्पुत्रो मुञ्चति**



**तस्मात्पुत्रो नाम स पुत्रेणेवास्मिल्ँ लोके प्रतितिष्ठत्यथैनमेते देवाः प्राणा अमृता आविशन्ति॥१७॥**

 अथ Next, now अतः hence सम्प्रत्तिः the right of giving (handing over, entrusting). यदा When मन्यते (a father) thinks प्रैष्यन् going to die अथ then आह (he) says इति thus पुत्रम् to the son त्वम् you ब्रह्मः (are) Brahman. त्वम् You यज्ञः (are) the sacrifice त्वम् you लोकः (are) the world. सः That पुत्रः son प्रत्याह says in reply इति thus. अहम् I ब्रह्म (am) Brahman. अहम् I यज्ञः (am) the sacrifice. अहम् I लोकः (am) the world. (The father) इति (thinks) thus वै verily यत् किं च whatever अनूक्तम् read from the preceptor एकता oneness, identity तस्य of that सर्वस्य all ब्रह्म (is) in the word “Brahman.” वै Verily ये के च whatever यज्ञाः sacrifices (are there) एकता oneness तेषाम् of them सर्वेषाम् all यज्ञः इति (is) in the word “sacrifice.” वै Verily ये के च whatever लोकाः worlds (are there) एकता oneness तेषाम् of them सर्वेषाम् all, लोकः इति (is) in the word “worid.” एतावत् So much वै indeed इदम् this सर्वम् all (study of the Vedas, performance of sacrifice, and attainment of worlds). अयम् Не सन् bеing एतत् this सर्वम् all अभुनजत् gets, obtains, protects मा इति me. तस्मात् For this reason आहुः (they) say अनुशिष्टम् instructed पुत्रम् son (is) लोक्यम् means of attaining the world, conducive to the world. तस्मात् Thence अनुशासति (a father) instructs एनम् him ( his son). यदा When सः he (the father) एवंविद् who knows thus प्रेति goes out, departs अस्मात् from this लोकात् world. अथ Then आविशति enters, penetrates एव verily पुत्रम् the son सह with एभिः these प्राणैः organs. यदि If



सः he अनेन by him अशक्त्या through weakness, through slip किं चित् any (is) अकृतम् not done, omitted तस्मात् from that सर्वस्मात् all that पुत्रः the son मुञ्चति releases, exonerates एनम् him. तस्मात् Therefore (he is) नाम called पुत्रः son. सः He प्रतितिष्ठति remains, continues अस्मिन् in this लोके world एव verily पुत्रेण through the son. अथ And एते these दैवाः divine अमृताः immortal प्राणाः organs (speech, mind and vital force) आविशन्ति enter, permeate एनम् him.

 Now follows the rite of the handing over. When a father thinks on account of some omen that he is going to depart, he calls his son and says to him, ‘you are Brahman, you are the sacrifice and you are the world.’ The son thus addressed by the father says in reply: ‘I am Brahman, I am the sacrifice, I am the world. The father thinks whatever is, has been, should be read from the preceptor becomes one in the word, “Brahman”. Similarly whatever sacrifices there were to be performed by me become one in the word, “sacrifice.” And whatever worlds there were to be attained by me become one in the word, “world.” The study of the Vedas, the performance of the sacrifices and attainment of worlds are the duties of a house-holder. The son by doing all these duties will save me from this world. Therefore the Brāhmans say that an instructed son is the means of attaining world for his father. Hence a father instructs his



son about his duties. When a father who has handed over his duties to his son leaves this world, he pervades his son together with the speech, the mind and the vital power. If any duty is omitted by the father through any weakness or oversight, the son saves him from all that omission by doing it himself. Therefore he is called son. The father although dead is immortal and continues to remain in this world through such a son. Divine and immortal speech, mind and vital power pertaining to Hiranyagarbha enter the father who has done so.

——————————————————————————————

\[NOTES—1. It is so called because the father in this way hands over his own duties to his son.

2\. Let the study of the Vedas, which was so long my duty, be yours.

3\. Let whatever sacrifices I used to do and was to be done by me be done by you.

4\. By you. From now you attain the world that was to be attained by me, whether I have attained them or not.

5\. The derivative meaning of the word ‘Putra’ is—“one who saves his father by completing his omissions.”\]

——————————————————————————————

 **पृथिव्यै चैनमग्नेश्च दैवी वागाविशति सा वै दैवी वाग्यया यद्यदेव वदति तत्तद्भवति॥१८॥**

 दैवी The divine, relating to gods वाक् speech पृथिव्यै from the earth च and अग्नेः from fireआविशति च enters एनं च



him. वै Verily सा that (is) दैवी divine, pure, free from evils वाक् speech यया by which यत् यत् whatever एव only वन्दति (he) says तत् तत् that (and) that भवति comes to pass, is fulfilled, becomes infallible and irresistible.

 The speech relating to the gods enters into him from the earth and fire. That divine speech consisting of earth and fire is pure and free from the evils of falsehood, etc. By that speech whatever he says about himself or others come to pass infallibly.

——————————————————————————————

\[NOTES—1. He who having entrusted his own duties to his son, performs rites and knows the meditation on three kinds of food as identical with himself.

2\. It is the material of vocal organs of all. In an ignorant man the divine speech is limited by attachment and other evils pertaining to the body. But this speech becomes all-pervading like water, or the unobstructed light of a lamp in a sage on account of his freedom from these evils.\]

——————————————————————————————

 **दिवश्चैनमादित्याच्च दैवं मन आविशति तद्वै दैवं मनो येनाऽऽनन्द्येव भवत्यथो न शोचति॥१९॥**

 दैवम् The divine मनः mind दिवः from heaven च and आदित्यात् from the sun आविशति च enters एनम् him. वै Verily that (is) दैवम् divine, pure, free from evils मनः mind येन by which भवति becomes आनन्दी joyful एव only अथ and उ surely न not शोचति grieves, mourns.



 The mind relating to the gods enters into him from heaven and the sun. That divine mind is naturally pure and free from evils. By that mind he becomes joyful and never grieves being away from the causes of grief.

 ** अद्भ्यश्चैनं चन्द्रमसश्च दैवः प्राण आविशति स वै दैवः प्राणो यः सञ्चरꣳश्चासञ्चरꣳश्च न व्यथतेऽथो न रिष्यति स एवंवित्सर्वेषां भूतानामात्मा भवति यथैषा देवतैवꣳस यथैतां देवताꣳ सर्वाणि भूतान्यवन्त्येवꣳ हैवंविदꣳ सर्वाणि भूतान्यवन्ति। यदु किञ्चेमाः प्रजाः शोचन्त्यमैवाऽऽसां तद्भवति पुण्यमेवामुं गच्छति न ह वै देवान्पापं गच्छति॥२०॥**

 दैवः The divine, relating to gods प्राणः life, the vital power अद्भ्यः न from water च and चन्द्रमसः from the moon आविशति enters, permeates एनम् this one, him. वै Verily सः that (is) दैवः divine प्राणः vital power यः which सञ्चरन् moving च and असञ्चरन् standing still, not moving न not व्यथते feels pain. अथ उ Therefore न not रिष्यति dies, is injured सः he एवंवित् who knows thus भवति becomes आत्मा the self सर्वेषाम् of all भूतानाम् beings. अथ As (is) एषा this देवता deity (Hiranyagarbha) एवम् so (is) सः he (the knower) यथा as सर्वाणि all भूतानि beings अवन्ति protects, worships एताम् this देवताम् deity (Hiranyagarbha) एवम् so सर्वाणि all भूतानि beings अवन्ति protects, worship ह indeed एवंविदम् such a knower (sage) यत् उ anything किं च whatever इमाः these, ordinary प्रजाः beings mortals शोचन्ति grieve अमाः that (grief)



एव verily आसाम् of these भवति is due to, comes from तत् it (its cause) पुण्यम् good results (merits) एव only गच्छति goes, approaches अमूम् to him. वै Verily पापम् evil results, demerits, ह ever न not गच्छति approaches, goes देवान् to the gods.

 Likewise vital power relating to gods enters him from water and the moon. That is the divine vital power which, moving in animals and standing still in stationary objects is neither pained nor injured nor killed. He who knows the meditation on three varieties of food as described above becomes the self of all beings. As is Hiranyagarbha who first realised this state, so is this knower. As Hiranyagarbha is worshipped through sacrifices, etc., by all beings so is this sage constantly worshipped by them. Whatever grief ordinary mortals suffer from that grief is due to their identification with limited things. But only the good results approach the sage who enjoys the status of Hiranyagarbha. No evil result i.e., the misery due to them approaches the gods.

——————————————————————————————

\[NOTES—1. Their vital power, mind and speech.

2\. His omniscience or omnipotence is not thwarted.\]

——————————————————————————————

 **अथातो व्रतमीमाꣳसा प्रजापतिर्ह कर्माणि ससृजे तानि सृष्टान्यन्योन्येनास्पर्धन्त वदिष्याम्येवाहमिति वाग्दध्रे द्रक्ष्याम्यह-**



**मिति चक्षुः श्रोष्याम्यहमिति श्रोत्रमेवमन्यानि कर्माणि यथाकर्म तानि मृत्युः श्रमो भूत्वोपयेमे तान्याप्नोत्तान्याप्त्वा मृत्युरवारुन्ध तस्माच्छ्राम्यत्येव वाक्श्राम्यति चक्षुः श्राम्यति श्रोत्रमथेममेव नाऽऽप्नोद्योऽयं मध्यमः प्राणस्तानि ज्ञातुं दध्रिरे। अयं वै नः श्रेष्ठो यः सञ्चरꣳश्चासञ्चरꣳश्च न व्यथतेऽथो न रिष्यति हन्तास्यैव सर्वे रूपमसामेति त एतस्यैव सर्वे रूपमभवꣳस्तस्मादेत एतेनाऽऽख्यायन्ते प्राणा इति तेन ह वाव तत्कुलमाचक्षते यस्मिन्कुले भवति य एवं वेद य उ हैवंविदा स्पर्धतेऽनुशुष्यत्यनुशुष्य हैवान्ततो म्रियत इत्यध्यात्मम्॥२१॥**

 अथः Next, now अत therefore ब्रत-मीमांसा consideration of the vow, discussion of observances. प्रजापतिः Prajapati, Viraj ससृजे created कर्माणि works, organs, तानि these सृष्टानि being created अस्पर्धन्तः vied, competed अन्यः one अन्येन with another, वाक् a speech दध्रे took a vow—made up (his) mind इति thus अहम् I एव only वदिष्यामि will speak. चक्षुः The eye इति (vowed) thus अहम् I द्रक्ष्यामि will see. श्रोत्रम् The ear इति (vowed) thus अहम् I श्रोष्यामि will hear. एवम् So, thus अन्यानि other कर्माणि works, organs (did) यथा-कर्म according to (their) functions. मृत्युः Death भूत्वा being, becoming श्रमः fatigue, tedium उपयेमे got, captured तानि them, आप्नोत् overwhelmed, overtook तानि them, आप्त्वा having overtaken, having overwhelmed तानि them (the organs) मृत्युः death अवारुन्द्ध obstructed, controlled. तस्मात् Therefore वाक् speech एव verily श्राम्यति gets tired, becomes fatigued,



चक्षुः the eye श्राम्यति becomes exhausted, श्रोत्रम् the ear श्राम्यति gets tired. अथ But प्राणः the vital power यः who मध्यमः (is) central, chief न not आप्नोत् overtook इमम् him, तानि these (organs) दध्रिरे resolved, made up minds ज्ञातुम् to know (it) वै एव verily अयम् this (is) श्रेष्ठः best, foremost नः among us यः who सञ्चरन् moving to and fro च and असञ्चरन् not moving न not व्यथते feels pain.अथ उ Therefore न not रिष्यति dies, is injured हन्त well सर्वे all (of us) एव indeed आसाम् let be, let assume अस्य his रुपम् इति form. ते They सर्वे all अभवन् became, assumed, identified with एतस्य his रुपम् form एव only. तस्मात् Therefore एते they अख्यायन्ते are called प्राणाः Pranas, Vital powers एतेन by this (name). तत् That कुलम् family यस्मिन् in, which कुले family भवति is born यः (he) who वेद knows एवम् thus ह indeed आचक्षते is spoken of, is named तेन after him बाब it is well-known यः उ who स्पर्धते ह competes, vies एवंविदा with such a knower (the Sage) अनुशुष्यति dries, shrivels. अनुशुष्य ह After shrivelling अन्ततः in the end म्रियते dies एव indeed इति this अध्यात्मम् (is) with reference to the body.

 Next begins a discussion of observances among the organs. Viraj created the works (organs¹). These organs after coming into existence competed with one another to observe their functions as duty. The organ of speech resolved to keep at his function of speaking. Similarly the eye made up his mind to go on seeing. The ear vowed to do his duty of hearing. Likewise did the other organs according to their respective functions. Death,



the destroyer, seized the organs in the form of tedium. It overwhelmed them and having overwhelmed them obstructed their functions. Therefore the speech cannot but be exhausted. So does the eye. And so does the ear. But death in the form of fatigue could not affect the vital power who is the chief in the body and functions in the mouth. The other organs made up their minds to know the vital power. They knew it to be the foremost among them, because when it moves to and fro, or does not move at all it feels no pain nor dies. Well, let us now assume its form. After this decision they all identified them with it and realised it as their own self. Hence they are known by the name of 'Prān.' That family in which a person is born who knows the organs as forms of the vital power is indeed called² after him by the people. And he who vies as a rival with the sage who has realised his identity with the vital force dries in this very body and after becoming dry dies at the end. This much is with regard to the body.

——————————————————————————————

\[NOTES—1.They are so called on account of being instruments of work.

2.The family is known after the name of this sage as the line of Tapati, the daughter of the sun, is called after her.  
—Anandagiri.\]

——————————————————————————————



 **अथाधिदैवतं ज्वलिष्याम्येवाहमित्यग्निर्दध्रे तप्स्याम्यहमित्यादित्यो भास्याम्यहमिति चन्द्रमा एवमन्या देवता यथादैवत^(ꣳ) स यथैषां प्राणानां मध्यमः प्राण एवमेतासां देवतानां वायुर्निर्म्लोचन्ति ह्यन्या देवता न वायुः सैषाऽनस्तमिता देवता यद्वायुः॥२२॥**

 अथ Now अधिदैवतम् (meditation) regarding the deities. इति Thus अग्निः fire दध्रे resolved vowed अहम् I एव only ज्वलिष्यामि will burn, आदित्यः the sun इति (resolved) thus: अहम् I तप्स्यामि will warm चन्द्रमाः the moon इति (vowed) thus: अहम् I भास्यामि will shine. एवम् Similarly अन्याः other देवताः gods, deities यथा दैवतम् according to functions, यथा as सः that प्राणः life vital power मध्यमः central, chief एषाम् of these प्राणानाम् vital forces, organs एवम् so वायुः Vayu, air एतासाम् of these देवानाम् gods, deities अन्याः other देबताः gods, deities निम्लोचन्ति cease to function, sink न not वायुः Vayu. सा That एषा this देवता god यत् which (is) वायुः Vayu, air न not अस्तम् इता declined, sets.

 Now the meditation regarding the deities. Fire resolved to burn. The sun held to warm. The moon took a vow to shine. And so did the other deities resolve in accordance with their respective duties. As the life^(1) is the chief of these organs in the body, so is Vayu (air) among these deities, such as fire. Other deities cease to function like the organ of speech, etc., but Vayu does



not like the vital power in the body. Therefore Vayu is the deity that never declines.

——————————————————————————————

 \[NOTES—1. It is not overtaken by death, nor stopped from functioning. His vow remains unbroken.\]

——————————————————————————————

 **अथैष श्लोको भवति यतश्चोदेति सूर्योऽस्तं यत्र च गच्छतीति प्राणाद्वा एष उदेति प्राणेऽस्तमेति तं देवाश्चक्रिरे धर्म^(ꣳ) स एवाद्य स उ श्व इति यद्वा एतेऽमूर्ह्यध्रियन्त तदेवाप्यद्य कुर्वन्ति। तस्मादेकमेव व्रतं चरेत् प्राण्याच्चैवापान्याच्च नेन्मा पाप्मा मृत्युराप्नुवदिति यद्युचरेत्समापिपयिषेत्तेनो एतस्यै देवतायै सायुज्य^(ꣳ) सलोकतां जयति॥२३॥ इति पञ्चमं ब्राह्मणम्॥५॥**

 अथ Hence. Therefore एषः this श्लोकः verse, mantra भवति there is—यतः च from which सूर्यः the Sun उदेति rises, यत्र in which च and अस्तं गच्छति इति goes down, sets वै verily एषः this (Sun) उदेति rises प्राणात् from the vital power अस्तम् एति goes down, disappears प्राणे in the vital power. देवाः The gods (such as fire) चक्रिरे made, observed धर्मम् religious duty, vow तम् of that (air and vital power) सः it, the vow (is) एव indeed अद्य to-day, now सः उ it (the vow) (is) श्वः इति to-morrow, in future यत् वा what (vow) एते these (gods) अध्रियन्त held, settled अमूर्हि then तत् that एव only कुर्वन्ति do, observe अद्य अपि to this day, even now. तस्मात् Therefore चरेत् (one) should observe, should adopt एव only एकम् a single व्रतम् vow, observance प्राण्यात् च do the function of Prana, do respiration च and अपान्यात् do the function of



Apan, do excretion चेत् lest पाप्माः evil मृत्युः death श्राप्नुवत् should seize, should reach मा इति me (him); यदि उ if चरेत् (he) observes (it) समापिषायिषेत् (he) should try to the last, should seek to finish तेन उ by it (vow) जयति conquers, attains सायुज्यम् union, identity, सलोकताम् existence in the same world एतस्यै with this देवतायै deity (vital power).

 Hence there is this Mantra: In ancient times fire and other gods as well as speech, etc., in the body observed the vow of air and the vital power. Externally the sun rises from air and internally from the vital power in the body as the eye. It sets in the air in the evening and when a man goes to sleep.¹ The vow is observed by the gods now. and will be observed in future by them. They follow now and will follow unbroken afterwards. Therefore a person should follow a single observance, a single vow—perform respiration and excretion, lest the evil of death should seize him in the form of fatigue. And if he takes up the vow of the vital force, he should try it to the last. By this vow he attains union with the vital force (whose cosmic form is Hiranyagarbha) or gets existence in the same world with this deity.

——————————————————————————————

 \[NOTES—1. When one sleeps, his speech, eye, etc., are all merged in the vital power and when one awakes, these again arise from it.\]

——————————————————————————————



 **त्रयं वा इदं नाम रूपं कर्म तेषां नाम्नां वागित्येतदेषामुक्थमथो हि सर्वाणि नामान्युत्तिष्ठन्ति। एतदेष^(ꣳ) सामैतद्धि सर्वैर्नामभिः सममेतदेषां ब्रह्मैतद्धि सर्वाणि नामानि बिभर्ति॥१॥**

 वै Verily इदम् this (universe) त्रयम् (is of) the three a triad—नाम name रुपम् form कर्म work, action. तेषाम् of those एषाम् these नाम्नाम् names एतत् this वाक् speech, sound in general. उक्थम् इति (is) the Uktha, cause, foundation हि for सर्वाणि all नामानि names particular sounds उत्तिष्ठति spring forth, rise अतः from it. एतत् It (is) एषाम् their साम Sāman, sameness, common feature हि for एतत् it (is) समम् common, general सर्वैः to all नामभिः names; एतत् it (is) एषाम् their ब्रह्म Brahman, Self, हि for एतत् it विभर्ति sustains, upholds सर्वाणि all नामानि names, particular sounds.

 Verily this Universe is made up of a triad: name, form and work—all non–self¹. Sound in general is the foundation of those names set forth before. For all particular names, (such as Yajnadatta and Devadatta) rise from it like particles of salt from the salt rock. It is their sameness, for it is same to all names which are nothing but its own particular forms. It is their Self, for it upholds all names by giving them reality.

——————————————————————————————

 \[NOTES—1. One should be averse to not–self—this Universe of name, form and action; and turn his gaze inward and

——————————————————————————————



see the inner Self. This is the import of this section. One whose mind is not averse to this not–self cannot have the inclination to meditate on the self. For the two tendencies of mind, one going outward and to the not–self and the other inclined to the inner self, are contradictory.\]

 **अथ रूपाणां चक्षुरित्येतदेषामुक्थमतो हि सर्वाणि रूपाण्युत्तिष्ठन्त्येतदेषा^(ꣳ) सामैतद्धि सर्वै रूपैः सममेतदेषां ब्रह्मैतद्धि सर्वाणि रूपाणि बिभर्ति॥२॥**

 अथ Now रुपाणाम् of forms (black, white etc) चक्षुः the eye, form in general, visible objects, इति एतत् it उक्थम् (is) the Uktha, source, material एषाम् of them, हि for अतः from it उत्तिष्ठन्ति spring forth, rise र्साणि all रूपाणि (particular) forms. एतत् It (is) एषाम् their साम (is) Saman, sameness हि for एतत् it समम् common सर्वै to all रूपैः forms; एतत् it (is) एषाम् their ब्रह्म Brahman, Self; हि for एतत् it बिभर्ति supports, sustains सर्वाणि all रूपाणि (particular ) forms.

 Now of forms, white, black, etc. Form in general is the cause of all particular forms, for all kinds of forms visible to the eye are born of it. It is their sameness. For it is the same to all particular forms. It is their self, for it upholds all kinds of forms.

 **अथ कर्मणामात्मेत्येतदेषामुक्थमतो हि सर्वाणि कर्माण्युत्तिष्ठन्त्येतदेषां^(ꣳ) सामैतद्धि सर्वैः कर्मभिः सममेतदेषां ब्रह्मैतद्धि सर्वाणि कर्माणि बिभर्ति तदेतत् त्रय^(ꣳ) सदेकमयमात्माऽऽत्मो एकः**



**सन्नेतत्त्रयं तदेतदमृत^(ꣳ) सत्त्येन च्छन्नं प्राणो वा अमृतं नामरूपे सत्त्यं ताभ्यामयं प्राणश्छन्नः॥३॥ इति षष्ठं ब्राह्मणम्॥६॥ इति प्रथमोऽध्यायः॥१॥**

 अथ Now एषाम् of these कर्मणाम् actions एतत् this आत्मा body, activity in general उक्थम् इति (is) Uktha, foundation, source, हि for सर्वाणि all कर्माणि (particular) actions उत्तिष्ठन्ति spring forth, rise अतः from it; एतत् it (is) एषाम् their साम Saman, sameness, हि for एतत् it समम् (is)
common, same, सर्वैः to all कर्मभिः (particular) actions एतत् it (is) एषाम् their ब्रह्म Brahman, Self हि for एतत् it बिभर्ति sustains, upholds सर्वाणि all कर्माणि (particular) actions. तत् That एतत् this त्रयम् trial सन् being एकम् one अयम् this आत्मा body, उ again आत्मा the body सन् being एकः one (is) एतत् this त्रयम् triad; तत् That एतत् this अमृतम् deathless one छन्नम् (is) hidden, covered by सत्येन Satya; verily प्राणः life, the subtle body consisting of organs (is) अमृतम् immortal नाम–रुपे the name and form (are) सत्यम् Satya, gross body, five elements ताभ्याम् by both अयम् this प्राणः life, subtle body, छन्नम् (is) covered, concealed.

 Now activity in general having its seat in the body is the source of all particular actions. For all such actions rise from it. It is their sameness; for it is same to all particular actions. It is their self; for it upholds all particular actions. These three, name, form and action (like three sticks supporting one another) are one–this body and



this body alone. Although one it is these three. The deathless one is hidden by satya (gross body), the subtle body is the deathless one¹; and name and form represented by gross body are satya²; so this subtle body³ is hidden by them.

——————————————————————————————

 \[NOTES—1. Subtle body survives the gross body, and is immortal in the sense that it is destroyed only by the knowledge of Brahman.—Nityananda.

 2. Satya literally means truth. But it is used here in a technical sense. Anandagiri and Nityananda explain the word as five elements—earth, water, air, fire and sky—of which the body is composed. Sureswara in his Vartika and Vidyaranya in his 'Vartikasara' and Maheswara in his Tika on 'Vartikasara' make these unanimous observations on this word: "Satya is what is called cosmic gross body that envelopes Hiranyagarbha or cosmic (collective) subtle body (consisting of seventeen instruments, five sense–organs, five organs of action, five vital forces, mind and intellect), which again covers the innermost (Supreme) Self.

 3. Subtle body supports the gross body as the pillars support a house from within.—Vidyaranya.\]

——————————————————————————————

CHAPTER TWO: SECTION ONE

 **ॐ दृप्तबालाकिर्हानूचानो गार्ग्य आस स होवाचाजातशत्रुं काश्यं ब्रह्म ते ब्रवाणीति स होवाचाजातशत्रुः सहस्रमेतस्यां वाचि दद्मो जनको जनक इति वै जना धावन्तीति॥१॥**



ॐ Om आस ह there was गार्ग्यः descendant of Gargya family दृप्त–बालाकिः the proud son of Balaki अनूचानः a skilled expounder, an eloquent speaker (of the Vedas). सः ह He उवाच said अजातशत्रुं to Ajatshatru काश्यम् King of Kashi (Benares) ब्रवाणि इति (I) will tell (teach) ते you ब्रह्म about Brahman. सः ह That अजातशत्रुः Ajatshatru उवाच said एतस्यां for this वाचि speech, statement दद्ये (I) give, offer (you) सहस्रं a thousand (cows) वै verily जनाः people धावन्ति run, rush जनकः जनकः इति (saying) 'Janak' 'Janak.'

 \[Knowledge of Brahman is greatly abstruse. To facilitate understanding it is presented here in the form of the following story. The story also teaches necessary rules of conduct between the teacher and the taught. If that condition is fulfilled, understanding of truth becomes possible. It is shown therein that understanding is impossible by mere arguments or logic–chopping. Faith is a great factor in the realisation of truth as evidenced in the story.\]

 Om. There was an eloquent expounder of the Vedas in the past. He was the proud son of Balākā and a descendant of Garga. He told Ajatshatru, King of Benares, that he would teach him about Brahman. For that kind statement Ajatshatru offered him a thousand cows. It is well known that people who want to hear or speak about Brahman run to Janaka, saying "he is benevolent, and he likes to hear about Brahman".



 ** स होवाच गार्ग्यो य एवासावादित्ये पुरुष एतमेवाहं ब्रह्मोपास इति स होवाचाजातशत्रुर्मा मैतस्मिन्संवदिष्ठा अतिष्ठाः सर्वेषां भूतानां मूर्धा राजेति वा अहमेतमुपास इति स य एतमेवमुपास्तेऽतिष्ठाः सर्वेषां भूतानां मूर्धा राजा भवति॥२॥**

 सः ह That गार्ग्यः Gargya, a descendant from Gargya family उवाच said आसौ that पुरुषः being यः who (is) एव indeed आदित्ये in the sun अहम् I उपासे meditate on, look upon एतम् him एव only ब्रह्म इति (as) Brahman. सः ह That अजातशत्रुः Ajatshatru मा not सम्बदिष्ठाः talk, speak एतस्मिन् about him वै verily अहम् I उपासे इति meditate, look एतम् upon it अतिष्ठाः (as) all– surpassing, supreme मूर्धा the head सर्वेषां of all भूतानां beings राजा इति (as) King endowed with resplendence सः ह he यः ह who उपास्ते meditates—upon, adores एतम् him एतम् as such भवति is, becomes अतिष्ठाः all–sur–passing, supreme मूर्धा the head सर्वेषां of all भूतानां beings राजा (and) King, resplendent.

 The descendant of Garga family said—'I adore as Brahman that Being who is identified with the sun and entering the body through the eye resides in the heart as ego^(1.') Ajatshatru replied—"Please do not speak to me about him as Brahman. Verily I adore him as the Supreme One. He is the head of all beings and is endowed with resplendence. He who adores him as such becomes^(2) supreme and the head of all beings and resplendent."



——————————————————————————————

\[NOTES—1. The agent and experiencer in these aggregate of body and organs.

 2. Shatapath Brahmana (10.5.2.20) rightly says: 'One becomes exactly as one meditates upon Him'.\]

——————————————————————————————

 **स होवाच गार्यो य एवासौ चन्द्रे पुरुष एतमेवाहं ब्रह्मोपास इति स होवाचाजातशत्रुर्मा मैतस्मिन्संवदिष्ठा बृहन्पाण्डरवासाः सोमो राजेति वा अहमेतमुपास इति स य एतमेवमुपास्तेऽहरर्ह सुतः प्रसुतो भवति नास्यान्नं क्षीयते॥३॥**

 सः ह That गार्ग्यः Gargya उवाच said असौ that पुरुषः being यः who (is) एव indeed चन्द्रे in the moon अहम् I उपासे meditate upon, adore एतम् him ब्रह्म इति (as) Brahman. सः ह That श्रजातशत्रुः Ajatshatru उवाच said मा not मा not संवदिष्ठाः talk, speak एतस्मिन् about him. वै Verily अहम् I उपासे इति meditate एतम् upon him बृहत् (as) the great पाण्डरवासाः white robed, clad in white raiment राजा इति King, radiant सोमः Soma. सः He चः who उपास्ते meditates upon, adores, एतम् him एवम् as such श्रहः श्रहः day by day भवति ह gets (sufficient soma) सतः poured out प्रसुतः pressed, poured forth one sacrifices); अस्य his अन्नः food न not क्षीयते fails, gets short.

 Gargya said—"That Being who is identified with the moon and is also in the mind I adore as Brahman.” At this, Ajatshatru requested him not to speak about him as Brahman and added, "I adore him as the great white–clad¹ radiant Soma. He who adores him with the above–mentioned



attributes gets sufficient soma in sacrifices. He is never short of food as he meditates upon Brahman as consisting of food."

——————————————————————————————

 \[NOTES—1. Because the vital power which is identified with the moon has got an aqueous body.\]

——————————————————————————————

 ** स होवाच गार्ग्यो य एवासौ विद्युति पुरुष एतमेवाहं ब्रह्मोपास इति स होवाचाजातशत्रुर्मा मैतस्मिन्संवदिष्ठास्तेजस्वीति वा अहमेतमुपास इति स य एतमेवमुपास्ते तेजस्वी ह भवति च तेजस्विनी हास्य प्रजा भवति॥४॥**

 सः ह That गार्ग्यः Gargya उवाच said असौ this पुरुषः being यः who ( is) एव indeed विद्युति in the lightning अहम् I उपासे meditate एतम् upon him ब्रह्म इति (as) Brahmin एव verily. सः ह That अजातशत्रुः Ajatshatru. उवाच said मा not मा not संवदिष्ठाः talk, speak एतस्मिन् about him. अहम् I वै verily उपासे meditate एतम् upon him तेजस्वी इति (as) luminous, powerful. सः He चः who उपास्ते meditates एतम् upon, him (that being) एवम् as such ह indeed भवति is, becomes तेजस्वी luminous, powerful. अस्य His प्रजा progeney ह indeed भवति becomes तेजस्विनी powerful.

 Gargya said—"I adore as Brahman that Being who is identified with the lightning and is in the skin and the heart." Ajatsatru said—"Do not speak to me about him as Brahman". Verily I adore him as luminous. He who adores that Being



with the above–mentioned attribute becomes luminous indeed. The result of the meditation reaches his progeny as well.

 ** स होवाच गार्ग्यो य एवायमाकाशे पुरुष एतमेवाहं ब्रह्मोपास इति स होवाचाजातशत्रुर्मा मैतस्मिन्संवदिष्ठाः पूर्णमप्रवर्तीति वा अहमेतमुपास इति स य एतमेवमुपास्ते पूर्यते प्रजया पशुभिर्नास्यास्माल्लोकात्प्रजोद्वर्तते॥५॥**

 सः ह That गार्ग्यः Gargya उवाच said अयम् this पुरुषः being यः who एव indeed आकाशे (is) in the ether. अहम् I उपासे meditate, adore एतम् upon him एव indeed ब्रह्म इति (as) Brahman. सः ह That अजातशत्रुः Ajatshatru उवाच said मा not मा not संवदिष्टाः talk, speak एतस्मिन् about him, अहम् I वै verily उपासे meditate एतम् इति upon him (that being) पूर्णम् (as) full अप्रवर्ति इति (as) unmoving, immobile. सः He यः who उपास्ते meditates एवम् upon it स्वम् as such पूर्यति is full एव indeed प्रजया of progeny पशभिः of cattle. अस्य His प्रजा progeny न not उद्वर्तते ceases, is extinct अस्मात् from this लोकात् world.

 Gārgya said—"I adore that Being as Brahman who is identified with the ether enclosed by the heart." Ajatshatru said—"Please do not speak to me about him as Brahman. Verily I adore that Being as full and immobile. He who adores that Being with these attributes  
becomes full of



progeny and cattle and the continuity of his line is preserved in this world."

 ** स होवाच गार्ग्यो य एवायं वायौ पुरुष एतमेवाहं ब्रह्मोपास इति स होवाचाजातशत्रुर्मा मैतस्मिन्संवदिष्ठा इन्द्रो वैकुण्ठोऽपराजिता सेनेति वा अहमेतमुपास इति स य एतमेवमुपास्ते जिष्णुर्हापराजिष्णुर्भवत्यन्यतस्त्यजायी॥६॥**

 सः ह That गार्ग्यः Gargya उवाच said अयं this पुरुषः being यः who एव indeed वायौ (is) in the air अहम् I उपासे meditate upon, adore एव verily एतम् him ब्रह्म इति (as) Brahman. सः ह That अजातशत्रु Ajatshatru उवाच said मा not मा not संवदिष्ठाः talk, speak एतस्मिन् about him अहम् I वै verily उपासे meditate upon, adore एतम् इति him इन्द्रः (as) the lord वैकुण्ठः (as) the irreisstible अपराजिता (as) the unvanquished, undefeated सेना इति Army. सः He यः who उपास्ते Meditates एतम् upon him एवं thus, as such ह ever भवति becomes जिष्णुः Victorious, अपराजिष्णुः unconquerable, invincible अन्यतस्त्यजायी conquer or of enemies.

 Gārgya said—'This Being who is identified with the air and is in the vital power and the heart I adore as Brahman.' Ajatshatru said—Please do not speak to me about him as Brahman. Verily I adore him as the Lord, the irresistible, the undefeated army^(1). He who adores that Being with these attributes, ever becomes victorious and unconquerable as well as the conqueror of his enemies.'



—————————————————————————————— 

 \[NOTES—1. Because Maruts who are the air–gods are a group.\]

——————————————————————————————

 ** स होवाच गार्ग्यो य एवायमग्नौ पुरुष एतमेवाहं ब्रह्मोपास इति स होवाचाजातशत्रुर्मा मैतस्मिन्संवदिष्ठा विषासहिरिति वा अहमेतमुपास इति स य एतमेवमुपास्ते विषासहिर्ह भवति विषासहिर्हास्य प्रजा भवति॥७॥**

 सः ह That गार्ग्यः Gargya उवाच said अयम् this पुरुषः Being यः who (is) एव indeed अग्नौ in the fire अहम् I उपासे meditate upon, adore एवम् him एव verily ब्रह्म इति (as) Brahman. सः ह That अजातशत्रुः Ajatshatru उवाच said मा not मा not संवादिष्ठाः talk, speak एतस्मिन् about him. अहम् I उपासे इति meditate वै verily एतम् upon him (that being) विषासहिः इति (as) tolerant, forbearing. सः He यः who उपास्ते meditates upon, adores एतम् him एव indeed भवति becomes ह ever विषासहिः tolerant, forbearing अस्य this प्रजा progeny ह too भवति becomes विसाषहिः forbearing, tolerant.

 Gārgya said—"This Being who is identified with fire and is in the speech and the heart I adore as Brahman." Ajatshatru said—"Please do not speak to me about him as Brahman. Verily I adore him as tolerant. He who adores him with these attributes becomes tolerant and his progeny too becomes tolerant."

 **स होवाच गार्ग्यो य एवायमप्सु पुरुष एतमेवाहं ब्रह्मोपास इति स होवाचाजातशत्रुर्मा मैतस्मिन्संवदिष्ठाः प्रतिरूप इति वा**



**अहमेतमुपास इति स य एतमेवमुपास्ते प्रतिरूप^(ꣳ) हैवैनमुपगच्छति नाप्रतिरूपमथो प्रतिरूपोऽस्माज्जायते॥८॥**

 सः ह That गार्ग्यः Gargya उवाच said अयम् this पुरुषः being यः who (is) एव indeed अप्सु in the water अहम् I उपासे meditate upon, adore एतम् him एव indeed ब्रह्म इति (as) Brahman. सः ह That अजातशत्रुः Ajatshatru उवाच said मा not मा not संवदिष्ठाः talk, speak एतस्मिन् about him. अहम् I verily उपासे meditate upon, adore एतम् him प्रतिरूपः इति (as) agreeable, not contrary. सः He यः who उपास्ते meditates upon, adores एतम् him एवम् as such अप्रतिरूपम् not adverse, not contrary (ones) अथ उ also अस्मात् from him प्रतिरूपः the agreeable (children) जायते are born.

 Gārgya said—"This Being who is identified with the water and is in the seed and the heart I adore as Brahman." Ajatshatru said—" Please do not speak to me about him as Brahman. Verily I adore him as not contrary to the Shrutis and Smritis. He who adores him with these attributes only agreeable things come to him, and not adverse ones. From him are born children who obey the scriptures.”

 **स होवाच गार्ग्यो य एवायमादर्शे पुरुष एतमेवाहं ब्रह्मोपास इति स होवाचाजातशत्रुर्मा मैतस्मिन्संवदिष्ठा रोचिष्णुरिति वा अहमेतमुपास इति स य एतमेवमुपास्ते रोचिष्णुई भवति**



**रोचिष्णुर्हास्य प्रजा भवत्यथो यैः सन्निगच्छति सर्वा^(ꣳ)स्तानतिरोचते॥९॥**

 सः ह That गार्ग्यः Gargya उवाच said अयम् this पुरुषः being यः who (is) एव indeed आदर्शे in the looking glass अहम् I उपासे meditate upon, adore एतम् him एव indeed ब्रह्म इति (as) Brahman. सः ह That अजातशत्रुः Ajatshatru उवाच said मा not मा not संवदिष्ठाः talk, speak एतस्मिन् about him. वै verily अहम् I उपासे इति meditate upon, adore एतम् him रोचिष्णुः (as) shining, bright. सः He यः who उपास्ते meditate एतम् upon him एवम् as such ह indeed भवति becomes रोचिष्णुः shining, bright अथ उ also सन्निगच्छति (he) out shines सर्वान् all तान् those यैः with whom अतिरोचते (he) comes in contact.

 Gārgya said—"This Being who is identified with the looking–glass and other shining objects (such as sword) and the intellect, I adore as Brahman." Ajatshatru said—"Please do not speak to me about him as Brahman. Verily I adore him as naturally bright. He who adores that Being with these attributes becomes bright and his progeny too becomes bright. He outshines all those whom he contacts."

 **स होवाच गार्ग्यो य एवायं यन्तं पश्चाच्छब्दोऽनूदेत्येतमेवाहं ब्रह्मोपास इति स होवाचाजातशत्रुर्मा मैतस्मिन्संवदिष्ठा**



**असुरिति वा अहमेतमुपास इति स य एतमेवमुपास्ते सर्व^(ꣳ) हैवास्मिल्ँ लोक आयुरेति नैनं पुरा कालात्प्राणो जहाति॥१०॥**
